  37:     /**
  38:      * PHP Error
  39:      * 
  40:      * --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- ---
  41:      * 
  42:      * WARNING! It is downright _DANGEROUS_ to use this in production, on
  43:      * a live website. It should *ONLY* be used for development.
  44:      * 
  45:      * PHP Error will kill your environment at will, clear the output
  46:      * buffers, and allows HTML injection from exceptions.
  47:      * 
  48:      * In future versions it plans to do far more then that.
  49:      * 
  50:      * If you use it in development, awesome! If you use it in production,
  51:      * you're an idiot.
  52:      * 
  53:      * --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- ---
  54:      * 
  55:      * = Info
  56:      * 
  57:      * A small API for replacing the standard PHP errors, with prettier
  58:      * error reporting. This will change the error reporting level, and this
  59:      * is deliberate, as I believe in strict development errors.
  60:      * 
  61:      * simple usage:
  62:      * 
  63:      *      \php_error\reportErrors();
  64:      * 
  65:      * Advanced example:
  66:      * 
  67:      * There is more too it if you want more customized error handling. You
  68:      * can pass in options, to customize the setup, and you get back a
  69:      * handler you can alter at runtime.
  70:      * 
  71:      *      $handler = new \php_error\ErrorHandler( $myOptions );
  72:      *      $handler->turnOn();
  73:      * 
  74:      * There should only ever be one handler! This is an (underdstandable)
  75:      * limitation in PHP. It's because if an exception or error is raised,
  76:      * then there is a single point of handling it.
  77:      * 
  78:      * = INI Options
  79:      * 
  80:      * - php_error.force_disabled When set to a true value (such as on),
  81:      *                            this forces this to be off.
  82:      *                            This is so you can disable this script
  83:      *                            in your production servers ini file,
  84:      *                            incase you accidentally upload this there.
  85:      * 
  86:      * --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- ---
  87:      * 
  88:      * @author Joseph Lenton | https://github.com/josephlenton
  89:      */
  90: 
  91:     namespace php_error;
  92: 
  93:     use \php_error\ErrorException,
  94:         \php_error\FileLinesSet,
  95:         \php_error\ErrorHandler,
  96: 
  97:         \php_error\JSMin,
  98:         \php_error\JSMinException;
  99: 
 100:     use \Closure,
 101:         \Exception,
 102:         \InvalidArgumentException;
 103: 
 104:     use \ReflectionMethod,
 105:         \ReflectionFunction,
 106:         \ReflectionParameter;
 107: 
 108:     global $_php_error_already_setup,
 109:            $_php_error_global_handler,
 110:            $_php_error_is_ini_enabled;
 111: 
 112:     /*
 113:      * Avoid being run twice.
 114:      */
 115:     if ( empty($_php_error_already_setup) ) {
 116:         $_php_error_already_setup = true;
 117: 
 118:         /*
 119:          * These are used as token identifiers by PHP.
 120:          * 
 121:          * If they are missing, then they should never pop out of PHP,
 122:          * so we just give them their future value.
 123:          * 
 124:          * They are primarily here so I don't have to alter the 5.3
 125:          * compliant code. Instead I can delete pre-5.3 code (this
 126:          * code), in the future.
 127:          * 
 128:          * As long as the value is unique, and does not clash with PHP,
 129:          * then any number could be used. That is why they start counting
 130:          * at 100,000.
 131:          */
 132:         if ( ! defined('T_DIR') ) {
 133:             define( 'T_DIR', 100001 );
 134:         }
 135:         if ( ! defined('T_GOTO') ) {
 136:             define( 'T_GOTO', 100002 );
 137:         }
 138:         if ( ! defined('T_NAMESPACE') ) {
 139:             define( 'T_NAMESPACE', 100003 );
 140:         }
 141:         if ( ! defined('T_NS_C') ) {
 142:             define( 'T_NS_C', 100004 );
 143:         }
 144:         if ( ! defined('T_NS_SEPARATOR') ) {
 145:             define( 'T_NS_SEPARATOR', 100005 );
 146:         }
 147:         if ( ! defined('T_USE') ) {
 148:             define( 'T_USE', 100006 );
 149:         }
 150: 
 151:         /*
 152:          * Check if it's empty, in case this file is loaded multiple times.
 153:          */
 154:         if ( ! isset($_php_error_global_handler) ) {
 155:             $_php_error_global_handler = null;
 156: 
 157:             $_php_error_is_ini_enabled = false;
 158: 
 159:             /*
 160:              * check both 'disable' and 'disabled' incase it's mispelt
 161:              * check that display errors is on
 162:              * and ensure we are *not* a command line script.
 163:              */
 164:             $_php_error_is_ini_enabled = 
 165:                     ! @get_cfg_var( 'php_error.force_disabled' ) &&
 166:                     ! @get_cfg_var( 'php_error.force_disable'  ) &&
 167:                       @ini_get('display_errors') === '1'         &&
 168:                        PHP_SAPI !== 'cli'
 169:             ;
 170:         }
 171: 
 172:         /**
 173:          * This is shorthand for turning off error handling,
 174:          * calling a block of code, and then turning it on.
 175:          * 
 176:          * However if 'reportErrors' has not been called,
 177:          * then this will silently do nothing.
 178:          * 
 179:          * @param callback A PHP function to call.
 180:          * @return The result of calling the callback.
 181:          */
 182:         function withoutErrors( $callback ) {
 183:             global $_php_error_global_handler;
 184: 
 185:             if ( $_php_error_global_handler !== null ) {
 186:                 return $_php_error_global_handler->withoutErrors( $callback );
 187:             } else {
 188:                 return $callback();
 189:             }
 190:         }
 191: 
 192:         /**
 193:          * Turns on error reporting, and returns the handler.
 194:          * 
 195:          * If you just want error reporting on, then don't bother
 196:          * catching the handler. If you're building something
 197:          * clever, like a framework, then you might want to grab
 198:          * and use it.
 199:          * 
 200:          * Note that calling this a second time will replace the
 201:          * global error handling with a new error handler.
 202:          * The existing one will be turned off, and the new one
 203:          * turned on.
 204:          * 
 205:          * You can't use two at once!
 206:          * 
 207:          * @param options Optional, options declaring how PHP Error should be setup and used.
 208:          * @return The ErrorHandler used for reporting errors.
 209:          */
 210:         function reportErrors( $options=null ) {
 211:             $handler = new ErrorHandler( $options );
 212:             return $handler->turnOn();
 213:         }
 214: 
 215:         /**
 216:          * The actual handler. There can only ever be one.
 217:          */
 218:         class ErrorHandler
 219:         {
 220:             const REGEX_DOCTYPE = '/<( )*!( *)DOCTYPE([^>]+)>/';
 221: 
 222:             const REGEX_PHP_IDENTIFIER = '\b[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*';
 223:             const REGEX_PHP_CONST_IDENTIFIER = '/\b[A-Z_\x7f-\xff][A-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*/';
 224: 
 225:             /**
 226:              * Matches:
 227:              *  {closure}()
 228:              *  blah::foo()
 229:              *  foo()
 230:              * 
 231:              * It is:
 232:              *      a closure
 233:              *      or a method or function
 234:              *      followed by parenthesis '()'
 235:              * 
 236:              *      a function is 'namespace function'
 237:              *      a method is 'namespace class::function', or 'namespace class->function'
 238:              *      the whole namespace is optional
 239:              *          namespace is made up of an '\' and then repeating 'namespace\'
 240:              *          both the first slash, and the repeating 'namespace\', are optional
 241:              * 
 242:              * 'END' matches it at the end of a string, the other one does not.
 243:              */
 244:             const REGEX_METHOD_OR_FUNCTION_END = '/(\\{closure\\})|(((\\\\)?(\b[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*\\\\)*)?\b[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*(::[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*)?)\\(\\)$/';
 245:             const REGEX_METHOD_OR_FUNCTION     = '/(\\{closure\\})|(((\\\\)?(\b[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*\\\\)*)?\b[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*(::[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*)?)\\(\\)/';
 246: 
 247:             const REGEX_VARIABLE = '/\b[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*$/';
 248: 
 249:             const REGEX_MISSING_SEMI_COLON_FOLLOWING_LINE = '/^ *(return|}|if|while|foreach|for|switch)/';
 250: 
 251:             /**
 252:              * The number of lines to take from the file,
 253:              * where the error is reported. This is the number
 254:              * of lines around the line in question,
 255:              * including that line.
 256:              * 
 257:              * So '9' will be the error line + 4 lines above + 4 lines below.
 258:              */
 259:             const NUM_FILE_LINES = 13;
 260: 
 261:             const FILE_TYPE_APPLICATION = 1;
 262:             const FILE_TYPE_IGNORE      = 2;
 263:             const FILE_TYPE_ROOT        = 3;
 264: 
 265:             const PHP_ERROR_MAGIC_HEADER_KEY = 'PHP_ERROR_MAGIC_HEADER';
 266:             const PHP_ERROR_MAGIC_HEADER_VALUE = 'php_stack_error';
 267:             const MAGIC_IS_PRETTY_ERRORS_MARKER = '<!-- __magic_php_error_is_a_stack_trace_constant__ -->';
 268: 
 269:             const PHP_ERROR_INI_PREFIX = 'php_error';
 270: 
 271:             /**
 272:              * At the time of writing, scalar type hints are unsupported.
 273:              * By scalar, I mean 'string' and 'integer'.
 274:              * 
 275:              * If they do get added, this is here as a trap to turn scalar
 276:              * type hint warnings on and off.
 277:              */
 278:             private static $IS_SCALAR_TYPE_HINTING_SUPPORTED = false;
 279: 
 280:             private static $SCALAR_TYPES = array(
 281:                     'string', 'integer', 'float', 'boolean',
 282:                     'bool', 'int', 'number'
 283:             );

 533:             private static function isIIS() {
 534:                 return (
 535:                                 isset($_SERVER['SERVER_SOFTWARE']) &&
 536:                                 strpos($_SERVER['SERVER_SOFTWARE'], 'IIS/') !== false
 537:                         ) || (
 538:                                 isset($_SERVER['_FCGI_X_PIPE_']) &&
 539:                                 strpos($_SERVER['_FCGI_X_PIPE_'], 'IISFCGI') !== false
 540:                         );
 541:             }
 542:             
 543:             /**
 544:              * This attempts to state if this is *not* a PHP request,
 545:              * but it cannot say if it *is* a PHP request. It achieves
 546:              * this by looking for a mime type.
 547:              *
 548:              * For example if the mime type is JavaScript, then we
 549:              * know it's not PHP. However there is no "yes, this is
 550:              * definitely a normal HTML response" flag we can check.
 551:              */
 552:             private static function isNonPHPRequest() {
 553:                 /*
 554:                  * Check if we are a mime type that isn't allowed.
 555:                  *
 556:                  * Anything other than 'text/html' or similar will cause
 557:                  * this to turn off.
 558:                  */
 559:                 $response = ErrorHandler::getResponseHeaders();
 560: 
 561:                 foreach ( $response as $key => $value ) {
 562:                     if ( strtolower($key) === 'content-type' ) {
 563:                         $found = true;
 564: 
 565:                         foreach ( ErrorHandler::$ALLOWED_RETURN_MIME_TYPES as $type ) {
 566:                             if ( stripos($value, $type) !== false ) {
 567:                                 $found = true;
 568:                                 break;
 569:                             }
 570:                         }
 571: 
 572:                         if ( ! $found ) {
 573:                             return true;
 574:                         }
 575: 
 576:                         break;
 577:                     }
 578:                 }
 579: 
 580:                 return false;
 581:             }
 582: 
 583:             /**
 584:              * Looks up a description for the symbol given,
 585:              * and if found, it is returned.
 586:              * 
 587:              * If it's not found, then the symbol given is returned.
 588:              */
 589:             private static function phpSymbolToDescription( $symbol ) {
 590:                 if ( isset(ErrorHandler::$PHP_SYMBOL_MAPPINGS[$symbol]) ) {
 591:                     return ErrorHandler::$PHP_SYMBOL_MAPPINGS[$symbol];
 592:                 } else {
 593:                     return "'$symbol'";
 594:                 }
 595:             }
 596: 
 597:             /**
 598:              * Attempts to syntax highlight the code snippet done.
 599:              * 
 600:              * This is then returned as HTML, ready to be dumped to the screen.
 601:              * 
 602:              * @param code An array of code lines to syntax highlight.
 603:              * @return HTML version of the code given, syntax highlighted.
 604:              */
 605:             private static function syntaxHighlight( $code ) {
 606:                 $syntaxMap = ErrorHandler::$syntaxMap;
 607: 
 608:                 // @supress invalid code raises a warning
 609:                 $tokens = @token_get_all( "<?php " . $code . " ?" . ">" );
 610:                 $html = array();
 611:                 $len = count($tokens)-1;
 612:                 $inString = false;
 613:                 $stringBuff = null;
 614:                 $skip = false;
 615: 
 616:                 for ( $i = 1; $i < $len; $i++ ) {
 617:                     $token = $tokens[$i];
 618: 
 619:                     if ( is_array($token) ) {
 620:                         $type = $token[0];
 621:                         $code = $token[1];
 622:                     } else {
 623:                         $type = null;
 624:                         $code = $token;
 625:                     }
 626: 
 627:                     // work out any whitespace padding
 628:                     if ( strpos($code, "\n") !== false && trim($code) === '' ) {
 629:                         if ( $inString ) {
 630:                             $html[]= "<span class='syntax-string'>" . join('', $stringBuff);
 631:                             $stringBuff = array();
 632:                         }
 633:                     } else if ( $code === '&' ) {
 634:                         if ( $i < $len ) {
 635:                             $next = $tokens[$i+1];
 636: 
 637:                             if ( is_array($next) && $next[0] === T_VARIABLE ) {
 638:                                 $type = 'reference_ampersand';
 639:                             }
 640:                         }
 641:                     } else if ( $code === '"' || $code === "'" ) {
 642:                         if ( $inString ) {
 643:                             $html[]= "<span class='syntax-string'>" . join('', $stringBuff) . htmlspecialchars($code) . "</span>";
 644:                             $stringBuff = null;
 645:                             $skip = true;
 646:                         } else {
 647:                             $stringBuff = array();
 648:                         }
 649: 
 650:                         $inString = !$inString;
 651:                     } else if ( $type === T_STRING ) {
 652:                         $matches = array();
 653:                         preg_match(ErrorHandler::REGEX_PHP_CONST_IDENTIFIER, $code, $matches);
 654: 
 655:                         if ( $matches && strlen($matches[0]) === strlen($code) ) {
 656:                             $type = 'const';
 657:                         }
 658:                     }
 659: 
 660:                     if ( $skip ) {
 661:                         $skip = false;
 662:                     } else {
 663:                         $code = htmlspecialchars( $code );
 664: 
 665:                         if ( $type !== null && isset($syntaxMap[$type]) ) {
 666:                             $class = $syntaxMap[$type];
 667: 
 668:                             if ( $type === T_CONSTANT_ENCAPSED_STRING && strpos($code, "\n") !== false ) {
 669:                                 $append = "<span class='$class'>" .
 670:                                             join(
 671:                                                     "</span>\n<span class='$class'>",
 672:                                                     explode( "\n", $code )
 673:                                             ) .
 674:                                         "</span>" ;
 675:                             } else if ( strrpos($code, "\n") === strlen($code)-1 ) {
 676:                                 $append = "<span class='$class'>" . substr($code, 0, strlen($code)-1) . "</span>\n";
 677:                             } else {
 678:                                 $append = "<span class='$class'>$code</span>";
 679:                             }
 680:                         } else if ( $inString && $code !== '"' ) {
 681:                             $append = "<span class='syntax-string'>$code</span>";
 682:                         } else {
 683:                             $append = $code;
 684:                         }
 685: 
 686:                         if ( $inString ) {
 687:                             $stringBuff[]= $append;
 688:                         } else {
 689:                             $html[]= $append;
 690:                         }
 691:                     }
 692:                 }
 693: 
 694:                 if ( $stringBuff !== null ) {
 695:                     $html[]= "<span class='syntax-string'>" . join('', $stringBuff) . '</span>';
 696:                     $stringBuff = null;
 697:                 }
 698: 
 699:                 return join( '', $html );
 700:             }
 701: 
 702:             /**
 703:              * Splits a given function name into it's 'class, function' parts.
 704:              * If there is no class, then null is returned.
 705:              * 
 706:              * It also returns these parts in an array of: array( $className, $functionName );
 707:              * 
 708:              * Usage:
 709:              * 
 710:              *      list( $class, $function ) = ErrorHandler::splitFunction( $name );
 711:              * 
 712:              * @param name The function name to split.
 713:              * @return An array containing class and function name.
 714:              */
 715:             private static function splitFunction( $name ) {
 716:                 $name = preg_replace( '/\\(\\)$/', '', $name );
 717: 
 718:                 if ( strpos($name, '::') !== false ) {
 719:                     $parts = explode( '::', $name );
 720:                     $className = $parts[0];
 721:                     $type = '::';
 722:                     $functionName = $parts[1];
 723:                 } else if ( strpos($name, '->') !== false ) {
 724:                     $parts = explode( '->', $name );
 725:                     $className = $parts[0];
 726:                     $type = '->';
 727:                     $functionName = $parts[1];
 728:                 } else {
 729:                     $className = null;
 730:                     $type = null;
 731:                     $functionName = $name;
 732:                 }
 733: 
 734:                 return array( $className, $type, $functionName );
 735:             }
 736: 
 737:             private static function newArgument( $name, $type=false, $isPassedByReference=false, $isOptional=false, $optionalValue=null, $highlight=false ) {
 738:                 if ( $name instanceof ReflectionParameter ) {
 739:                     $highlight = func_num_args() > 1 ?
 740:                             $highlight = $type :
 741:                             false;
 742: 
 743:                     $klass = $name->getDeclaringClass();
 744:                     $functionName = $name->getDeclaringFunction()->name;
 745:                     if ( $klass !== null ) {
 746:                         $klass = $klass->name;
 747:                     }
 748: 
 749:                     $export = ReflectionParameter::export(
 750:                             ( $klass ?
 751:                                     array( "\\$klass", $functionName ) :
 752:                                     $functionName ),
 753:                             $name->name, 
 754:                             true
 755:                     );
 756: 
 757:                     $paramType = preg_replace('/.*?(\w+)\s+\$'.$name->name.'.*/', '\\1', $export);
 758:                     if ( strpos($paramType, '[') !== false || strlen($paramType) === 0 ) {
 759:                         $paramType = null;
 760:                     }
 761: 
 762:                     return ErrorHandler::newArgument(
 763:                             $name->name,
 764:                             $paramType,
 765:                             $name->isPassedByReference(),
 766:                             $name->isDefaultValueAvailable(),
 767:                             ( $name->isDefaultValueAvailable() ?
 768:                                     var_export( $name->getDefaultValue(), true ) :
 769:                                     null ),
 770:                             ( func_num_args() > 1 ?
 771:                                     $type :
 772:                                     false )
 773:                     );
 774:                 } else {
 775:                     return array(
 776:                             'name'              => $name,
 777:                             'has_type'          => ( $type !== false ),
 778:                             'type'              => $type,
 779:                             'is_reference'      => $isPassedByReference,
 780:                             'has_default'       => $isOptional,
 781:                             'default_val'       => $optionalValue,
 782:                             'is_highlighted'    => $highlight
 783:                     );
 784:                 }
 785:             }
 786: 
 787:             private static function syntaxHighlightFunctionMatch( $match, &$stackTrace, $highlightArg=null, &$numHighlighted=0 ) {
 788:                 list( $className, $type, $functionName ) = ErrorHandler::splitFunction( $match );
 789: 
 790:                 // is class::method()
 791:                 if ( $className !== null ) {
 792:                     $reflectFun = new ReflectionMethod( $className, $functionName );
 793:                 // is a function
 794:                 } else if ( $functionName === '{closure}' ) {
 795:                     return '<span class="syntax-variable">$closure</span>';
 796:                 } else {
 797:                     $reflectFun = new ReflectionFunction( $functionName );
 798:                 }
 799: 
 800:                 if ( $reflectFun ) {
 801:                     $params = $reflectFun->getParameters();
 802: 
 803:                     if ( $params ) {
 804:                         $args = array();
 805:                         $min = 0;
 806:                         foreach( $params as $i => $param ) {
 807:                             $arg = ErrorHandler::newArgument( $param );
 808: 
 809:                             if ( ! $arg['has_default'] ) {
 810:                                 $min = $i;
 811:                             }
 812: 
 813:                             $args[]= $arg;
 814:                         }
 815: 
 816:                         if ( $highlightArg !== null ) {
 817:                             for ( $i = $highlightArg; $i <= $min; $i++ ) {
 818:                                 $args[$i]['is_highlighted'] = true;
 819:                             }
 820: 
 821:                             $numHighlighted = $min-$highlightArg;
 822:                         }
 823: 
 824:                         if ( $className !== null ) {
 825:                             if ( $stackTrace && isset($stackTrace[1]) && isset($stackTrace[1]['type']) ) {
 826:                                 $type = htmlspecialchars( $stackTrace[1]['type'] );
 827:                             }
 828:                         } else {
 829:                             $type = null;
 830:                         }
 831: 
 832:                         return ErrorHandler::syntaxHighlightFunction( $className, $type, $functionName, $args );
 833:                     }
 834:                 }
 835: 
 836:                 return null;
 837:             }
 838: 
 839:             /**
 840:              * Returns the values given, as HTML, syntax highlighted.
 841:              * It's a shorter, slightly faster, more no-nonsense approach
 842:              * then 'syntaxHighlight'.
 843:              * 
 844:              * This is for syntax highlighting:
 845:              *  - fun( [args] )
 846:              *  - class->fun( [args] )
 847:              *  - class::fun( [args] )
 848:              * 
 849:              * Class and type can be null, to denote no class, but are not optional.
 850:              */
 851:             private static function syntaxHighlightFunction( $class, $type, $fun, &$args=null ) {
 852:                 $info = array();
 853: 
 854:                 // set the info
 855:                 if ( isset($class) && $class && isset($type) && $type ) {
 856:                     if ( $type === '->' ) {
 857:                         $type = '-&gt;';
 858:                     }
 859: 
 860:                     $info []= "<span class='syntax-class'>$class</span>$type";
 861:                 }
 862: 
 863:                 if ( isset($fun) && $fun ) {
 864:                     $info []= "<span class='syntax-function'>$fun</span>";
 865:                 }
 866: 
 867:                 if ( $args ) {
 868:                     $info []= '( ';
 869: 
 870:                     foreach ($args as $i => $arg) {
 871:                         if ( $i > 0 ) {
 872:                             $info[]= ', ';
 873:                         }
 874: 
 875:                         if ( is_string($arg) ) {
 876:                             $info[]= $arg;
 877:                         } else {
 878:                             $highlight = $arg['is_highlighted'];
 879:                             $name = $arg['name'];
 880: 
 881:                             if ( $highlight ) {
 882:                                 $info[]= '<span class="syntax-higlight-variable">';
 883:                             }
 884: 
 885:                             if ( $name === '_' ) {
 886:                                 $info[]= '<span class="syntax-variable-not-important">';
 887:                             }
 888: 
 889:                             if ( $arg['has_type'] ) {
 890:                                 $info []= "<span class='syntax-class'>";
 891:                                     $info []= $arg['type'];
 892:                                 $info []= '</span> ';
 893:                             }
 894: 
 895:                             if ( $arg['is_reference'] ) {
 896:                                 $info []= '<span class="syntax-function">&amp;</span>';
 897:                             }
 898: 
 899:                             $info []= "<span class='syntax-variable'>\$$name</span>";
 900: 
 901:                             if ( $arg['has_default'] ) {
 902:                                 $info []= '=<span class="syntax-literal">' . $arg['default_val'] . '</span>';
 903:                             }
 904: 
 905:                             if ( $name === '_' ) {
 906:                                 $info[]= '</span>';
 907:                             }
 908:                             if ( $highlight ) {
 909:                                 $info[]= '</span>';
 910:                             }
 911:                         }
 912:                     }
 913: 
 914:                     $info []= ' )';
 915:                 } else {
 916:                     $info []= '()';
 917:                 }
 918: 
 919:                 return join( '', $info );
 920:             }
 921: 
 922:             /**
 923:              * Checks if the item is in options, and if it is, then it is removed and returned.
 924:              * 
 925:              * If it is not found, or if options is not an array, then the alt is returned.
 926:              */
 927:             private static function optionsPop( &$options, $key, $alt=null ) {
 928:                 if ( $options && isset($options[$key]) ) {
 929:                     $val = $options[$key];
 930:                     unset( $options[$key] );
 931: 
 932:                     return $val;
 933:                 } else {
 934:                     $iniAlt = @get_cfg_var( ErrorHandler::PHP_ERROR_INI_PREFIX . '.' . $key );
 935: 
 936:                     if ( $iniAlt !== false ) {
 937:                         return $iniAlt;
 938:                     } else {
 939:                         return $alt;
 940:                     }
 941:                 }
 942:             }
 943: 
 944:             private static function folderTypeToCSS( $type ) {
 945:                 if ( $type === ErrorHandler::FILE_TYPE_ROOT ) {
 946:                     return 'file-root';
 947:                 } else if ( $type === ErrorHandler::FILE_TYPE_IGNORE ) {
 948:                     return 'file-ignore';
 949:                 } else if ( $type === ErrorHandler::FILE_TYPE_APPLICATION ) {
 950:                     return 'file-app';
 951:                 } else {
 952:                     return 'file-common';
 953:                 }
 954:             }
 955: 
 956:             private static function isFolderType( &$folders, $longest, $file ) {
 957:                 $parts = explode( '/', $file );
 958: 
 959:                 $len = min( count($parts), $longest );
 960: 
 961:                 for ( $i = $len; $i > 0; $i-- ) {
 962:                     if ( isset($folders[$i]) ) {
 963:                         $folderParts = &$folders[ $i ];
 964: 
 965:                         $success = false;
 966:                         for ( $j = 0; $j < count($folderParts); $j++ ) {
 967:                             $folderNames = $folderParts[$j];
 968: 
 969:                             for ( $k = 0; $k < count($folderNames); $k++ ) {
 970:                                 if ( $folderNames[$k] === $parts[$k] ) {
 971:                                     $success = true;
 972:                                 } else {
 973:                                     $success = false;
 974:                                     break;
 975:                                 }
 976:                             }
 977:                         }
 978: 
 979:                         if ( $success ) {
 980:                             return true;
 981:                         }
 982:                     }
 983:                 }
 984: 
 985:                 return false;
 986:             }
 987: 
 988:             private static function setFolders( &$origFolders, &$longest, $folders ) {
 989:                 $newFolders = array();
 990:                 $newLongest = 0;
 991: 
 992:                 if ( $folders ) {
 993:                     if ( is_array($folders) ) {
 994:                         foreach ( $folders as $folder ) {
 995:                             ErrorHandler::setFoldersInner( $newFolders, $newLongest, $folder );
 996:                         }
 997:                     } else if ( is_string($folders) ) {
 998:                         ErrorHandler::setFoldersInner( $newFolders, $newLongest, $folders );
 999:                     } else {
1000:                         throw new Exception( "Unknown value given for folder: " . $folders );
1001:                     }
1002:                 }
1003: 
1004:                 $origFolders = $newFolders;
1005:                 $longest     = $newLongest;
1006:             }
1007: 
1008:             private static function setFoldersInner( &$newFolders, &$newLongest, $folder ) {
1009:                 $folder = str_replace( '\\', '/', $folder );
1010:                 $folder = preg_replace( '/(^\\/+)|(\\/+$)/', '', $folder );
1011:                 $parts  = explode( '/', $folder );
1012:                 $count  = count( $parts );
1013: 
1014:                 $newLongest = max( $newLongest, $count );
1015:                 
1016:                 if ( isset($newFolders[$count]) ) {
1017:                     $folds = &$newFolders[$count];
1018:                     $folds[]= $parts;
1019:                 } else {
1020:                     $newFolders[$count] = array( $parts );
1021:                 }
1022:             }
1023: 
1024:             private static function getRequestHeaders() {
1025:                 if ( function_exists('getallheaders') ) {
1026:                     return getallheaders();
1027:                 } else {
1028:                     $headers = array();
1029:                     
1030:                     foreach ( $_SERVER as $key => $value ) {
1031:                         if ( strpos($key, 'HTTP_') === 0 ) {
1032:                             $key = str_replace( " ", "-", ucwords(strtolower( str_replace("_", " ", substr($key, 5)) )) ); 
1033:                             $headers[ $key ] = $value;
1034:                         }
1035:                     }
1036: 
1037:                     return $headers;
1038:                 }
1039:             }
1040: 
1041:             private static function getResponseHeaders() {
1042:                 $headers = function_exists('apache_response_headers') ?
1043:                         apache_response_headers() :
1044:                         array() ;
1045: 
1046:                 /*
1047:                  * Merge the headers_list into apache_response_headers.
1048:                  * 
1049:                  * This is because sometimes things are in one, which are
1050:                  * not present in the other.
1051:                  */
1052:                 if ( function_exists('headers_list') ) {
1053:                     $hList = headers_list();
1054: 
1055:                     foreach ($hList as $header) {
1056:                         $header = explode(":", $header);
1057:                         $headers[ array_shift($header) ] = trim( implode(":", $header) );
1058:                     }
1059:                 }
1060: 
1061:                 return $headers;
1062:             }
1063: 
1064:             public static function identifyTypeHTML( $arg, $recurseLevels=1 ) {
1065:                 if ( ! is_array($arg) && !is_object($arg) ) {
1066:                     if ( is_string($arg) ) {
1067:                         return "<span class='syntax-string'>&quot;" . htmlentities($arg) . "&quot;</span>";
1068:                     } else {
1069:                         return "<span class='syntax-literal'>" . var_export( $arg, true ) . '</span>';
1070:                     }
1071:                 } else if ( is_array($arg) ) {
1072:                     if ( count($arg) === 0 ) {
1073:                         return "[]";
1074:                     } else if ( $recurseLevels > 0 ) {
1075:                         $argArr = array();
1076: 
1077:                         foreach ($arg as $ag) {
1078:                             $argArr[]= ErrorHandler::identifyTypeHTML( $ag, $recurseLevels-1 );
1079:                         }
1080: 
1081:                         if ( ($recurseLevels % 2) === 0 ) {
1082:                             return "["  . join(', ', $argArr) .  "]";
1083:                         } else {
1084:                             return "[ " . join(', ', $argArr) . " ]";
1085:                         }
1086:                     } else {
1087:                         return "[...]";
1088:                     }
1089:                 } else if ( get_class($arg) === 'Closure' ) {
1090:                     return '<span class="syntax-variable">$Closure</span>()';
1091:                 } else {
1092:                     $argKlass = get_class( $arg );
1093: 
1094:                     if ( preg_match(ErrorHandler::REGEX_PHP_CONST_IDENTIFIER, $argKlass) ) {
1095:                         return '<span class="syntax-literal">$' . $argKlass . '</span>';
1096:                     } else {
1097:                         return '<span class="syntax-variable">$' . $argKlass . '</span>';
1098:                     }
1099:                 }
1100:             }

1137: 
1138:             /**
1139:              * = Options =
1140:              * 
1141:              * All options are optional, and so is passing in an options item.
1142:              * You don't have to supply any, it's up to you.
1143:              * 
1144:              * Note that if 'php_error.force_disable' is true, then this object
1145:              * will try to look like it works, but won't actually do anything.
1146:              * 
1147:              * All options can also be passed in from 'php.ini'. You do this
1148:              * by setting it with 'php_error.' prefix. For example:
1149:              * 
1150:              *      php_error.catch_ajax_errors = On
1151:              *      php_error.error_reporting_on = E_ALL | E_STRICT
1152:              * 
1153:              * Includes:
1154:              *  = Types of errors this will catch =
1155:              *  - catch_ajax_errors         When on, this will inject JS Ajax wrapping code, to allow this to catch any future JSON errors. Defaults to true.
1156:              *  - catch_supressed_errors    The @ supresses errors. If set to true, then they are still reported anyway, but respected when false. Defaults to false.
1157:              *  - catch_class_not_found     When true, loading a class that does not exist will be caught. This defaults to true.
1158:              * 
1159:              *  = Error reporting level =
1160:              *  - error_reporting_on        value for when errors are on, defaults to all errors
1161:              *  - error_reporting_off       value for when errors are off, defaults to php.ini's error_reporting.
1162:              * 
1163:              *  = Setup Details =
1164:              *  - application_root          When it's working out hte stack trace, this is the root folder of the application, to use as it's base.
1165:              *                              Defaults to the servers root directory.
1166:              * 
1167:              *                              A relative path can be given, but lets be honest, an explicit path is the way to guarantee that you
1168:              *                              will get the path you want. My relative might not be the same as your relative.
1169:              * 
1170:              *  - snippet_num_lines         The number of lines to display in the code snippet. 
1171:              *                              That includes the line being reported.
1172:              * 
1173:              *  - server_name               The name for this server, defaults to "$_SERVER['SERVER_NAME']"
1174:              * 
1175:              *  - ignore_folders            This is allows you to highlight non-framework code in a stack trace.
1176:              *                              An array of folders to ignore, when working out the stack trace.
1177:              *                              This is folder prefixes in relation to the application_root, whatever that might be.
1178:              *                              They are only ignored if there is a file found outside of them.
1179:              *                              If you still don't get what this does, don't worry, it's here cos I use it.
1180:              * 
1181:              *  - application_folders       Just like ignore, but anything found in these folders takes precedence
1182:              *                              over anything else.
1183:              * 
1184:              *  - background_text           The text that appeares in the background. By default this is blank.
1185:              *                              Why? You can replace this with the name of your framework, for extra customization spice.
1186:              * 
1187:              *  - html_only                 By default, PHP Error only runs on ajax and HTML pages.
1188:              *                              If this is false, then it will also run when on non-HTML
1189:              *                              pages too, such as replying with images of JavaScript
1190:              *                              from your PHP. Defaults to true.
1191:              * 
1192:              * @param options Optional, an array of values to customize this handler.
1193:              * @throws Exception This is raised if given an options that does *not* exist (so you know that option is meaningless).
1194:              */
1195:             public function __construct( $options=null ) {
1196:                 // there can only be one to rule them all
1197:                 global $_php_error_global_handler;
1198:                 if ( $_php_error_global_handler !== null ) {
1199:                     $this->lastGlobalErrorHandler = $_php_error_global_handler;
1200:                 } else {
1201:                     $this->lastGlobalErrorHandler = null;
1202:                 }
1203:                 $_php_error_global_handler = $this;
1204: 
1205:                 $this->cachedFiles = array();
1206: 
1207:                 $this->isShutdownRegistered = false;
1208:                 $this->isOn = false;
1209: 
1210:                 /*
1211:                  * Deal with the options.
1212:                  * 
1213:                  * They are removed one by one, and any left, will raise an error.
1214:                  */
1215: 
1216:                 $ignoreFolders                  = ErrorHandler::optionsPop( $options, 'ignore_folders'     , null );
1217:                 $appFolders                     = ErrorHandler::optionsPop( $options, 'application_folders', null );
1218: 
1219:                 if ( $ignoreFolders !== null ) {
1220:                     ErrorHandler::setFolders( $this->ignoreFolders, $this->ignoreFoldersLongest, $ignoreFolders );
1221:                 }
1222:                 if ( $appFolders !== null ) {
1223:                     ErrorHandler::setFolders( $this->applicationFolders, $this->applicationFoldersLongest, $appFolders );
1224:                 }
1225: 
1226:                 $this->defaultErrorReportingOn  = ErrorHandler::optionsPop( $options, 'error_reporting_on' , -1 );
1227:                 $this->defaultErrorReportingOff = ErrorHandler::optionsPop( $options, 'error_reporting_off', error_reporting() );
1228: 
1229:                 $this->applicationRoot          = ErrorHandler::optionsPop( $options, 'application_root'   , $_SERVER['DOCUMENT_ROOT'] );
1230:                 $this->serverName               = ErrorHandler::optionsPop( $options, 'error_reporting_off', $_SERVER['SERVER_NAME']   );
1231: 
1232:                 /*
1233:                  * Relative paths might be given for document root,
1234:                  * so we make it explicit.
1235:                  */
1236:                 $dir = @realpath( $this->applicationRoot );
1237:                 if ( ! is_string($dir) ) {
1238:                     throw new Exception("Document root not found: " . $this->applicationRoot);
1239:                 } else {
1240:                     $this->applicationRoot =  str_replace( '\\', '/', $dir );
1241:                 }
1242: 
1243:                 $this->catchClassNotFound       = !! ErrorHandler::optionsPop( $options, 'catch_class_not_found' , true  );
1244:                 $this->catchSurpressedErrors    = !! ErrorHandler::optionsPop( $options, 'catch_supressed_errors', false );
1245:                 $this->catchAjaxErrors          = !! ErrorHandler::optionsPop( $options, 'catch_ajax_errors'     , true  );
1246: 
1247:                 $this->backgroundText           = ErrorHandler::optionsPop( $options, 'background_text'       , ''    );
1248:                 $this->numLines                 = ErrorHandler::optionsPop( $options, 'snippet_num_lines'     , ErrorHandler::NUM_FILE_LINES        );
1249:                 $this->displayLineNumber        = ErrorHandler::optionsPop( $options, 'display_line_numbers'  , false );
1250: 
1251:                 $this->htmlOnly                 = !! ErrorHandler::optionsPop( $options, 'html_only', true );
1252: 
1253:                 $this->classNotFoundException   = null;
1254: 
1255:                 $wordpress = ErrorHandler::optionsPop( $options, 'wordpress', false );
1256:                 if ( $wordpress ) {
1257:                     // php doesn't like | in constants and privates, so just set it directly : (
1258:                     $this->defaultErrorReportingOn = E_ERROR | E_WARNING | E_PARSE | E_USER_DEPRECATED & ~E_DEPRECATED & ~E_STRICT;
1259:                 }
1260: 
1261:                 if ( $options ) {
1262:                     foreach ( $options as $key => $val ) {
1263:                         throw new InvalidArgumentException( "Unknown option given $key" );
1264:                     }
1265:                 }
1266: 
1267:                 $this->isAjax =
1268:                         isset( $_SERVER['HTTP_X_REQUESTED_WITH'] ) &&
1269:                         ( $_SERVER['HTTP_X_REQUESTED_WITH'] === 'XMLHttpRequest' );
1270: 
1271:                 $this->isBufferSetup = false;
1272:                 $this->bufferOutputStr = '';
1273:                 $this->bufferOutput = false;
1274: 
1275:                 $this->startBuffer();
1276:             }
1277: 
1278:             /*
1279:              * --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- ---
1280:              * Public Functions
1281:              * --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- ---
1282:              */
1283: 
1284:             /**
1285:              * @return true if this is currently on, false if not.
1286:              */
1287:             public function isOn() {
1288:                 return $this->isOn;
1289:             }
1290: 
1291:             /**
1292:              * @return If this is off, this returns true, otherwise false.
1293:              */
1294:             public function isOff() {
1295:                 return !$this->isOn;
1296:             }
1297: 
1298:             /**
1299:              * Turns error reporting on.
1300:              * 
1301:              * This will use the strictest error reporting available, or the
1302:              * level you pass in when creating this using the 'error_reporting_on'
1303:              * option.
1304:              * 
1305:              * @return This error reporting handler, for method chaining.
1306:              */
1307:             public function turnOn() {
1308:                 $this->propagateTurnOff();
1309:                 $this->setEnabled( true );
1310: 
1311:                 return $this;
1312:             }
1313: 
1314:             /**
1315:              * Turns error reporting off.
1316:              * 
1317:              * This will use the 'php.ini' setting for the error_reporting level,
1318:              * or one you have passed in if you used the 'error_reporting_off'
1319:              * option when creating this.
1320:              * 
1321:              * @return This error reporting handler, for method chaining.
1322:              */
1323:             public function turnOff() {
1324:                 $this->setEnabled( false );
1325: 
1326:                 return $this;
1327:             }
1328: 
1329:             /**
1330:              * Allows you to run a callback with strict errors turned off.
1331:              * Standard errors still apply, but this will use the default
1332:              * error and exception handlers.
1333:              * 
1334:              * This is useful for when loading libraries which do not
1335:              * adhere to strict errors, such as Wordpress.
1336:              * 
1337:              * To use:
1338:              * 
1339:              *      withoutErrors( function() {
1340:              *          // unsafe code here
1341:              *      });
1342:              * 
1343:              * This will use the error_reporting value for when this is
1344:              * turned off.
1345:              * 
1346:              * @param callback A PHP function to call.
1347:              * @return The result of calling the callback.
1348:              */
1349:             public function withoutErrors( $callback ) {
1350:                 if ( ! is_callable($callback) ) {
1351:                     throw new Exception( "non callable callback given" );
1352:                 }
1353: 
1354:                 if ( $this->isOn() ) {
1355:                     $this->turnOff();
1356:                     $result = $callback();
1357:                     $this->turnOn();
1358: 
1359:                     return $result;
1360:                 } else {
1361:                     return $callback();
1362:                 }
1363:             }
1364:             
1365:             /**
1366:              * This is the shutdown function, which should *only* be called 
1367:              * via 'register_shutdown_function'.
1368:              * 
1369:              * It's exposed because it has to be exposed.
1370:              */
1371:             public function __onShutdown() {
1372:                 global $_php_error_is_ini_enabled;
1373:                 
1374:                 if ( $_php_error_is_ini_enabled ) {
1375:                     if ( $this->isOn() ) {
1376:                         $error = error_get_last();
1377: 
1378:                         // fatal and syntax errors
1379:                         if (
1380:                                 $error && (
1381:                                         $error['type'] ===  1 ||
1382:                                         $error['type'] ===  4 ||
1383:                                         $error['type'] === 64
1384:                                 )
1385:                         ) {
1386:                             $this->reportError( $error['type'], $error['message'], $error['line'], $error['file'] );
1387:                         } else {
1388:                             $this->endBuffer();
1389:                         }
1390:                     } else {
1391:                         $this->endBuffer();
1392:                     }
1393:                 }
1394:             }
1395: 
1396:             /*
1397:              * --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- ---
1398:              * Private Functions
1399:              * --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- --- ---
1400:              */
1401: 
1402:             private function propagateTurnOff() {
1403:                 if ( $this->lastGlobalErrorHandler !== null ) {
1404:                     $this->lastGlobalErrorHandler->turnOff();
1405:                     $this->lastGlobalErrorHandler->propagateTurnOff();
1406:                     $this->lastGlobalErrorHandler = null;
1407:                 }
1408:             }
1409:             
1410:             /**
1411:              * This is intended to be used closely with 'onShutdown'.
1412:              * It ensures that output buffering is turned on.
1413:              * 
1414:              * Why? The user may output content, and *then* hit an error.
1415:              * We cannot replace the page if this happens,
1416:              * because they have already outputted information.
1417:              * 
1418:              * So we buffer the page, and then output at the end of the page,
1419:              * or when an error strikes.
1420:              */
1421:             private function startBuffer() {
1422:                 global $_php_error_is_ini_enabled;
1423:                 
1424:                 if ( $_php_error_is_ini_enabled && !$this->isBufferSetup ) {
1425:                     $this->isBufferSetup = true;
1426: 
1427:                     ini_set( 'implicit_flush', false );
1428:                     ob_implicit_flush( false );
1429: 
1430:                     if ( ! @ini_get('output_buffering') ) {
1431:                         @ini_set( 'output_buffering', 'on' );
1432:                     }
1433: 
1434:                     $output = '';
1435:                     $bufferOutput = true;
1436: 
1437:                     $this->bufferOutputStr  = &$output;
1438:                     $this->bufferOutput = &$bufferOutput;
1439: 
1440:                     ob_start( function($string) use (&$output, &$bufferOutput) {
1441:                         if ( $bufferOutput ) {
1442:                             $output .= $string;
1443:                             return '';
1444:                         } else {
1445:                             $temp = $output . $string;
1446:                             $output = '';
1447:                             return $temp;
1448:                         }
1449:                     });
1450: 
1451:                     $self = $this;
1452:                     register_shutdown_function( function() use ( $self ) {
1453:                         $self->__onShutdown();
1454:                     });
1455:                 }
1456:             }
1457: 
1458:             /**
1459:              * Turns off buffering, and discards anything buffered
1460:              * so far.
1461:              * 
1462:              * This will return what has been buffered incase you
1463:              * do want it. However otherwise, it will be lost.
1464:              */
1465:             private function discardBuffer() {
1466:                 $str = $this->bufferOutputStr;
1467: 
1468:                 $this->bufferOutputStr = '';
1469:                 $this->bufferOutput = false;
1470: 
1471:                 return $str;
1472:             }
1473: 
1474:             /**
1475:              * Flushes the internal buffer,
1476:              * outputting what is left.
1477:              * 
1478:              * @param append Optional, extra content to append onto the output buffer.
1479:              */
1480:             private function flushBuffer() {
1481:                 $temp = $this->bufferOutputStr;
1482:                 $this->bufferOutputStr = '';
1483: 
1484:                 return $temp;
1485:             }
1486: 
1487:             /**
1488:              * This will finish buffering, and output the page.
1489:              * It also appends the magic JS onto the beginning of the page,
1490:              * if enabled, to allow working with Ajax.
1491:              * 
1492:              * Note that if PHP Error has been disabled in the php.ini file,
1493:              * or through some other option, such as running from the command line,
1494:              * then this will do nothing (as no buffering will take place).
1495:              */
1496:             public function endBuffer() {
1497:                 if ( $this->isBufferSetup ) {
1498:                     if ( 
1499:                             !$this->isAjax &&
1500:                              $this->catchAjaxErrors &&
1501:                             (!$this->htmlOnly || !ErrorHandler::isNonPHPRequest())
1502:                     ) {
1503:                         $content  = ob_get_contents();
1504:                         $handlers = ob_list_handlers();
1505: 
1506:                         $wasGZHandler = false;
1507: 
1508:                         $this->bufferOutput = true;
1509:                         for ( $i = count($handlers)-1; $i >= 0; $i-- ) {
1510:                             $handler = $handlers[$i];
1511: 
1512:                             if ( $handler === 'ob_gzhandler' ) {
1513:                                 $wasGZHandler = true;
1514:                                 ob_end_clean();
1515:                             } else if ( $handler === 'default output handler' ) {
1516:                                 ob_end_clean();
1517:                             } else {
1518:                                 ob_end_flush();
1519:                             }
1520:                         }
1521: 
1522:                         $content = $this->discardBuffer();
1523: 
1524:                         if ( $wasGZHandler ) {
1525:                             ob_start('ob_gzhandler');
1526:                         } else {
1527:                             ob_start();
1528:                         }
1529:            
1530:                         $js = $this->getContent( 'displayJSInjection' );
1531:                         $js = JSMin::minify( $js );
1532: 
1533:                         // attemp to inject the script into the HTML, after the doctype
1534:                         $matches = array();
1535:                         preg_match( ErrorHandler::REGEX_DOCTYPE, $content, $matches );
1536: 
1537:                         if ( $matches ) {
1538:                             $doctype = $matches[0];
1539:                             $content = preg_replace( ErrorHandler::REGEX_DOCTYPE, "$doctype $js", $content );
1540:                         } else {
1541:                             echo $js;
1542:                         }
1543:           
1544:                         echo $content;
1545:                     }
1546:                 }
1547:             }
1548: 
1549:             /**
1550:              * Calls the given method on this object,
1551:              * captures it's output, and then returns it.
1552:              * 
1553:              * @param method The name of the method to call.
1554:              * @return All of the text outputted during the method call.
1555:              */
1556:             private function getContent( $method ) {
1557:                 ob_start();
1558:                 $this->$method();
1559:                 $content = ob_get_contents();
1560:                 ob_end_clean();
1561: 
1562:                 return $content;
1563:             }
1564: 
1565:             private function isApplicationFolder( $file ) {
1566:                 return ErrorHandler::isFolderType(
1567:                         $this->applicationFolders,
1568:                         $this->applicationFoldersLongest,
1569:                         $file
1570:                 );
1571:             }
1572: 
1573:             private function isIgnoreFolder( $file ) {
1574:                 return ErrorHandler::isFolderType(
1575:                         $this->ignoreFolders,
1576:                         $this->ignoreFoldersLongest,
1577:                         $file
1578:                 );
1579:             }
1580: 
1581:             private function getFolderType( $root, $file ) {
1582:                 $testFile = $this->removeRootPath( $root, $file );
1583: 
1584:                 // it's this file : (
1585:                 if ( $file === __FILE__ ) {
1586:                     $type = ErrorHandler::FILE_TYPE_IGNORE;
1587:                 } else if ( strpos($testFile, '/') === false ) {
1588:                     $type = ErrorHandler::FILE_TYPE_ROOT;
1589:                 } else if ( $this->isApplicationFolder($testFile) ) {
1590:                     $type = ErrorHandler::FILE_TYPE_APPLICATION;
1591:                 } else if ( $this->isIgnoreFolder($testFile) ) {
1592:                     $type = ErrorHandler::FILE_TYPE_IGNORE;
1593:                 } else {
1594:                     $type = false;
1595:                 }
1596: 
1597:                 return array( $type, $testFile );
1598:             }
1599: 
1600:             /**
1601:              * Finds the file named, and returns it's contents in an array.
1602:              * 
1603:              * It's essentially the same as 'file_get_contents'. However
1604:              * this will add caching at this PHP layer, avoiding lots of
1605:              * duplicate calls.
1606:              * 
1607:              * It also splits the file into an array of lines, and makes
1608:              * it html safe.
1609:              * 
1610:              * @param path The file to get the contents of.
1611:              * @return The file we are after, as an array of lines.
1612:              */
1613:             private function getFileContents( $path ) {
1614:                 if ( isset($this->cachedFiles[$path]) ) {
1615:                     return $this->cachedFiles[$path];
1616:                 } else {
1617:                     $contents = @file_get_contents( $path );
1618: 
1619:                     if ( $contents ) {
1620:                         $contents = explode(
1621:                                 "\n",
1622:                                 preg_replace(
1623:                                         '/(\r\n)|(\n\r)|\r/',
1624:                                         "\n",
1625:                                         str_replace( "\t", '    ', $contents )
1626:                                 )
1627:                         );
1628: 
1629:                         $this->cachedFiles[ $path ] = $contents;
1630: 
1631:                         return $contents;
1632:                     }
1633:                 }
1634: 
1635:                 return array();
1636:             }
1637: 
1638:             /**
1639:              * Reads out the code from the section of the line,
1640:              * which is at fault.
1641:              * 
1642:              * The array is in a mapping of: array( line-number => line )
1643:              * 
1644:              * If something goes wrong, then null is returned.
1645:              */
1646:             private function readCodeFile( $errFile, $errLine ) {
1647:                 try {
1648:                     $lines = $this->getFileContents( $errFile );
1649: 
1650:                     if ( $lines ) {
1651:                         $numLines = $this->numLines;
1652: 
1653:                         $searchUp   = ceil( $numLines*0.75 );
1654:                         $searchDown = $numLines - $searchUp;
1655:                         
1656:                         $countLines = count( $lines );
1657: 
1658:                         /*
1659:                          * Search around the errLine.
1660:                          * We should aim get half of the lines above, and half from below.
1661:                          * If that fails we get as many as we can.
1662:                          */
1663: 
1664:                         /*
1665:                          * If we are near the bottom edge,
1666:                          * we go down as far as we can,
1667:                          * then work up the search area.
1668:                          */
1669:                         if ( $errLine+$searchDown > $countLines ) {
1670:                             $minLine = max( 0, $countLines-$numLines );
1671:                             $maxLine = $countLines;
1672:                         /*
1673:                          * Go up as far as we can, up to half the search area.
1674:                          * Then stretch down the whole search area.
1675:                          */
1676:                         } else {
1677:                             $minLine = max( 0, $errLine-$searchUp );
1678:                             $maxLine = min( $minLine+$numLines, count($lines) );
1679:                         }
1680: 
1681:                         $fileLines = array_splice( $lines, $minLine, $maxLine-$minLine );
1682: 
1683:                         $stripSize = -1;
1684:                         foreach ( $fileLines as $i => $line ) {
1685:                             $newLine = ltrim( $line, ' ' );
1686: 
1687:                             if ( strlen($newLine) > 0 ) {
1688:                                 $numSpaces = strlen($line) - strlen($newLine);
1689: 
1690:                                 if ( $stripSize === -1 ) {
1691:                                     $stripSize = $numSpaces;
1692:                                 } else {
1693:                                     $stripSize = min( $stripSize, $numSpaces );
1694:                                 }
1695:                             } else {
1696:                                 $fileLines[$i] = $newLine;
1697:                             }
1698:                         }
1699:                         if ( $stripSize > 0 ) {
1700:                             /*
1701:                              * It's pretty common that PHP code is not flush with the left hand edge,
1702:                              * so subtract 4 spaces, if we can,
1703:                              * to account for this.
1704:                              */
1705:                             if ( $stripSize > 4 ) {
1706:                                 $stripSize -= 4;
1707:                             }
1708: 
1709:                             foreach ( $fileLines as $i => $line ) {
1710:                                 if ( strlen($line) > $stripSize ) {
1711:                                     $fileLines[$i] = substr( $line, $stripSize );
1712:                                 }
1713:                             }
1714:                         }
1715: 
1716:                         $fileLines = join( "\n", $fileLines );
1717:                         $fileLines = ErrorHandler::syntaxHighlight( $fileLines );
1718:                         $fileLines = explode( "\n", $fileLines );
1719: 
1720:                         $lines = array();
1721:                         for ( $i = 0; $i < count($fileLines); $i++ ) {
1722:                             // +1 is because line numbers start at 1, whilst arrays start at 0
1723:                             $lines[ $i+$minLine+1 ] = $fileLines[$i];
1724:                         }
1725:                     }
1726: 
1727:                     return $lines;
1728:                 } catch ( Exception $ex ) {
1729:                     return null;
1730:                 }
1731: 
1732:                 return null;
1733:             }
1734: 
1735:             /**
1736:              * Attempts to remove the root path from the path given.
1737:              * If the path can't be removed, then the original path is returned.
1738:              * 
1739:              * For example if root is 'C:/users/projects/my_site',
1740:              * and the file is 'C:/users/projects/my_site/index.php',
1741:              * then the root is removed, and we are left with just 'index.php'.
1742:              * 
1743:              * This is to remove line noise; you don't need to be told the
1744:              * 'C:/whatever' bit 20 times.
1745:              * 
1746:              * @param root The root path to remove.
1747:              * @param path The file we are removing the root section from.
1748:              */
1749:             private function removeRootPath( $root, $path ) {
1750:                 $filePath = str_replace( '\\', '/', $path );
1751: 
1752:                 if (
1753:                         strpos($filePath, $root) === 0 &&
1754:                         strlen($root) < strlen($filePath)
1755:                 ) {
1756:                     return substr($filePath, strlen($root)+1 );
1757:                 } else {
1758:                     return $filePath;
1759:                 }
1760:             }
1761: 
1762:             /**
1763:              * Parses, and alters, the errLine, errFile and message given.
1764:              * 
1765:              * This includes adding syntax highlighting, removing duplicate
1766:              * information we already have, and making the error easier to
1767:              * read.
1768:              */
1769:             private function improveErrorMessage( $ex, $code, $message, $errLine, $errFile, $root, &$stackTrace ) {
1770:                 // change these to change where the source file is come from
1771:                 $srcErrFile = $errFile;
1772:                 $srcErrLine = $errLine;
1773:                 $altInfo = null;
1774:                 $stackSearchI = 0;
1775: 
1776:                 $skipStackFirst = function( &$stackTrace ) {
1777:                     $skipFirst = true;
1778: 
1779:                     foreach ( $stackTrace as $i => $trace ) {
1780:                          if ( $skipFirst ) {
1781:                               $skipFirst = false;
1782:                          } else {
1783:                               if ( $trace && isset($trace['file']) && isset($trace['line']) ) {
1784:                                    return array( $trace['file'], $trace['line'], $i );
1785:                               }
1786:                         }
1787:                     }
1788: 
1789:                     return array( null, null, null );
1790:                 };
1791: 
1792:                 /*
1793:                  * This is for calling a function that doesn't exist.
1794:                  * 
1795:                  * The message contains a long description of where this takes
1796:                  * place, even though we are already told this through line and
1797:                  * file info. So we cut it out.
1798:                  */
1799:                 if ( $code === 1 ) {
1800:                     if (
1801:                             ( strpos($message, " undefined method ") !== false ) ||
1802:                             ( strpos($message, " undefined function ") !== false )
1803:                     ) {
1804:                         $matches = array();
1805:                         preg_match( '/\b[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*((->|::)[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*)?\\(\\)$/', $message, $matches );
1806: 
1807:                         /*
1808:                          * undefined function or method call
1809:                          */
1810:                         if ( $matches ) {
1811:                             list( $className, $type, $functionName ) = ErrorHandler::splitFunction( $matches[0] );
1812: 
1813:                             if ( $stackTrace && isset($stackTrace[1]) && $stackTrace[1]['args'] ) {
1814:                                 $numArgs = count( $stackTrace[1]['args'] );
1815: 
1816:                                 for ( $i = 0; $i < $numArgs; $i++ ) {
1817:                                     $args[]= ErrorHandler::newArgument( "_" );
1818:                                 }
1819:                             }
1820: 
1821:                             $message = preg_replace(
1822:                                     '/\b[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*((->|::)[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*)?\\(\\)$/',
1823:                                     ErrorHandler::syntaxHighlightFunction( $className, $type, $functionName, $args ),
1824:                                     $message
1825:                             );
1826:                         }
1827:                     } else if ( $message === 'Using $this when not in object context' ) {
1828:                         $message = 'Using <span class="syntax-variable">$this</span> outside object context';
1829:                     /*
1830:                      * Class not found error.
1831:                      */
1832:                     } else if (
1833:                         strpos($message, "Class ") !== false &&
1834:                         strpos($message, "not found") !== false
1835:                     ) {
1836:                         $matches = array();
1837:                         preg_match( '/\'(\\\\)?[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*((\\\\)?[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*)+\'/', $message, $matches );
1838: 
1839:                         if ( count($matches) > 0 ) {
1840:                             // lose the 'quotes'
1841:                             $className = $matches[0];
1842:                             $className = substr( $className, 1, strlen($className)-2 );
1843: 
1844:                             $message = preg_replace(
1845:                                     '/\'(\\\\)?[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*((\\\\)?[a-zA-Z_\x7f-\xff][a-zA-Z0-9_\x7f-\xff]*)+\'/',
1846:                                     "<span class='syntax-class'>$className</span>",
1847:                                     $message
1848:                             );
1849:                         }
1850:                     }
1851:                 } else if ( $code === 2 ) {
1852:                     if ( strpos($message, "Missing argument ") === 0 ) {
1853:                         $message = preg_replace( '/, called in .*$/', '', $message );
1854: 
1855:                         $matches = array();
1856:                         preg_match( ErrorHandler::REGEX_METHOD_OR_FUNCTION_END, $message, $matches );
1857: 
1858:                         if ( $matches ) {
1859:                             $argumentMathces = array();
1860:                             preg_match( '/^Missing argument ([0-9]+)/', $message, $argumentMathces );
1861:                             $highlightArg = count($argumentMathces) === 2 ?
1862:                                     (((int) $argumentMathces[1])-1) :
1863:                                     null ;
1864: 
1865:                             $numHighlighted = 0;
1866:                             $altInfo = ErrorHandler::syntaxHighlightFunctionMatch( $matches[0], $stackTrace, $highlightArg, $numHighlighted );
1867: 
1868:                             if ( $numHighlighted > 0 ) {
1869:                                 $message = preg_replace( '/^Missing argument ([0-9]+)/', 'Missing arguments ', $message );
1870:                             }
1871: 
1872:                             if ( $altInfo ) {
1873:                                 $message = preg_replace( ErrorHandler::REGEX_METHOD_OR_FUNCTION_END, $altInfo, $message );
1874: 
1875:                                 list( $srcErrFile, $srcErrLine, $stackSearchI ) = $skipStackFirst( $stackTrace );
1876:                             }
1877:                         }
1878:                     } else if (
1879:                             strpos($message, 'require(') === 0 ||
1880:                             strpos($message, 'include(') === 0
1881:                     ) {
1882:                         $endI  = strpos( $message, '):' );
1883: 
1884:                         if ( $endI ) {
1885:                             // include( is the same length
1886:                             $requireLen = strlen('require(');
1887: 
1888:                             /*
1889:                              * +2 to include the ): at the end of the string
1890:                              */
1891:                             $postMessage = substr( $message, $endI+2 );
1892:                             $postMessage = str_replace( 'failed to open stream: No ', 'no ', $postMessage );
1893:                             $message = substr_replace( $message, $postMessage, $endI+2 );
1894: 
1895:                             /*
1896:                              * If this string is in there, and where we think it should be,
1897:                              * swap it with a shorter message.
1898:                              */
1899:                             $replaceBit = 'failed to open stream: No ';
1900:                             if ( strpos($message, $replaceBit) === $endI+2 ) {
1901:                                 $message  = substr_replace( $message, 'no ', $endI+2, strlen($replaceBit) );
1902:                             }
1903: 
1904:                             /*
1905:                              * Now put the string highlighting in there.
1906:                              */
1907:                             $match = substr( $message, $requireLen, $endI-$requireLen );
1908:                             $newString = "<span class='syntax-string'>'$match'</span>),";
1909:                             $message  = substr_replace( $message, $newString, $requireLen, ($endI-$requireLen)+2 );
1910:                         }
1911:                     }
1912:                 /*
1913:                  * Unexpected symbol errors.
1914:                  * For example 'unexpected T_OBJECT_OPERATOR'.
1915:                  * 
1916:                  * This swaps the 'T_WHATEVER' for the symbolic representation.
1917:                  */
1918:                 } else if ( $code === 4 ) {
1919:                     if ( $message === "syntax error, unexpected T_ENCAPSED_AND_WHITESPACE" ) {
1920:                         $message = "syntax error, string is not closed";
1921:                     } else {
1922:                         $semiColonError = false;
1923:                         if ( strpos($message, 'syntax error,') === 0 && $errLine > 2 ) {
1924:                             $lines = ErrorHandler::getFileContents( $errFile );
1925:                             
1926:                             $line = $lines[$errLine-1];
1927:                             if ( preg_match( ErrorHandler::REGEX_MISSING_SEMI_COLON_FOLLOWING_LINE, $line ) !== 0 ) {
1928:                                 $content = rtrim( join( "\n", array_slice($lines, 0, $errLine-1) ) );
1929: 
1930:                                 if ( strrpos($content, ';') !== strlen($content)-1 ) {
1931:                                     $message = "Missing semi-colon";
1932:                                     $errLine--;
1933:                                     $srcErrLine = $errLine;
1934:                                     $semiColonError = true;
1935:                                 }
1936:                             }
1937:                         }
1938: 
1939:                         if ( $semiColonError ) {
1940:                             $matches = array();
1941:                             $num = preg_match( '/\bunexpected ([A-Z_]+|\\$end)\b/', $message, $matches );
1942: 
1943:                             if ( $num > 0 ) {
1944:                                 $match = $matches[0];
1945:                                 $newSymbol = ErrorHandler::phpSymbolToDescription( str_replace('unexpected ', '', $match) );
1946: 
1947:                                 $message = str_replace( $match, "unexpected $newSymbol", $message );
1948:                             }
1949: 
1950:                             $matches = array();
1951:                             $num = preg_match( '/, expecting ([A-Z_]+|\\$end)( or ([A-Z_]+|\\$end))*/', $message, $matches );
1952: 
1953:                             if ( $num > 0 ) {
1954:                                 $match = $matches[0];
1955:                                 $newMatch = str_replace( ", expecting ", '', $match );
1956:                                 $symbols = explode( ' or ', $newMatch );
1957:                                 foreach ( $symbols as $i => $sym ) {
1958:                                     $symbols[$i] = ErrorHandler::phpSymbolToDescription( $sym );
1959:                                 }
