1960:                                 $newMatch = join( ', or ', $symbols );
1961: 
1962:                                 $message = str_replace( $match, ", expecting $newMatch", $message );
1963:                             }
1964:                         }
1965:                     }
1966:                 /**
1967:                  * Undefined Variable, add syntax highlighting and make variable from 'foo' too '$foo'.
1968:                  */
1969:                 } else if ( $code === 8 ) {
1970:                     if (
1971:                         strpos($message, "Undefined variable:") !== false
1972:                     ) {
1973:                         $matches = array();
1974:                         preg_match( ErrorHandler::REGEX_VARIABLE, $message, $matches );
1975: 
1976:                         if ( count($matches) > 0 ) {
1977:                             $message = 'Undefined variable <span class="syntax-variable">$' . $matches[0] . '</span>' ;
1978:                         }
1979:                     }
1980:                 /**
1981:                  * Invalid type given.
1982:                  */
1983:                 } else if ( $code === 4096 ) {
1984:                     if ( strpos($message, 'must be an ') ) {
1985:                         $message = preg_replace( '/, called in .*$/', '', $message );
1986: 
1987:                         $matches = array();
1988:                         preg_match( ErrorHandler::REGEX_METHOD_OR_FUNCTION, $message, $matches );
1989: 
1990:                         if ( $matches ) {
1991:                             $argumentMathces = array();
1992:                             preg_match( '/^Argument ([0-9]+)/', $message, $argumentMathces );
1993:                             $highlightArg = count($argumentMathces) === 2 ?
1994:                                     (((int) $argumentMathces[1])-1) :
1995:                                     null ;
1996: 
1997:                             $fun = ErrorHandler::syntaxHighlightFunctionMatch( $matches[0], $stackTrace, $highlightArg );
1998: 
1999:                             if ( $fun ) {
2000:                                 $message = str_replace( 'passed to ', 'calling ', $message );
2001:                                 $message = preg_replace( ErrorHandler::REGEX_METHOD_OR_FUNCTION, $fun, $message );
2002:                                 $prioritizeCaller = true;
2003: 
2004:                                 /*
2005:                                  * scalars not supported.
2006:                                  */
2007:                                 $scalarType = null;
2008:                                 if ( ! ErrorHandler::$IS_SCALAR_TYPE_HINTING_SUPPORTED ) {
2009:                                     foreach ( ErrorHandler::$SCALAR_TYPES as $scalar ) {
2010:                                         if ( stripos($message, "must be an instance of $scalar,") !== false ) {
2011:                                             $scalarType = $scalar;
2012:                                             break;
2013:                                         }
2014:                                     }
2015:                                 }
2016: 
2017:                                 if ( $scalarType !== null ) {
2018:                                     $message = preg_replace( '/^Argument [0-9]+ calling /', 'Incorrect type hinting for ', $message );
2019:                                     $message = preg_replace(
2020:                                             '/ must be an instance of ' . ErrorHandler::REGEX_PHP_IDENTIFIER . '\b.*$/',
2021:                                             ", ${scalarType} is not supported",
2022:                                             $message
2023:                                     );
2024: 
2025:                                     $prioritizeCaller = false;
2026:                                 } else {
2027:                                     $message = preg_replace( '/ must be an (instance of )?' . ErrorHandler::REGEX_PHP_IDENTIFIER . '\b/', '', $message );
2028: 
2029:                                     if ( preg_match('/, none given$/', $message) ) {
2030:                                         $message = preg_replace( '/^Argument /', 'Missing argument ', $message );
2031:                                         $message = preg_replace( '/, none given$/', '', $message );
2032:                                     } else {
2033:                                         $message = preg_replace( '/^Argument /', 'Incorrect argument ', $message );
2034:                                     }
2035:                                 }
2036: 
2037:                                 if ( $prioritizeCaller ) {
2038:                                     list( $srcErrFile, $srcErrLine, $stackSearchI ) = $skipStackFirst( $stackTrace );
2039:                                 }
2040:                             }
2041:                         }
2042:                     }
2043:                 }
2044: 
2045:                 if ( $stackTrace !== null ) {
2046:                     $isEmpty = count( $stackTrace ) === 0 ;
2047: 
2048:                     if ( $isEmpty ) {
2049:                         array_unshift( $stackTrace, array(
2050:                                 'line' => $errLine,
2051:                                 'file' => $errFile
2052:                         ) );
2053:                     } else if (
2054:                             count($stackTrace) > 0 && (
2055:                                     (! isset($stackTrace[0]['line'])) ||
2056:                                     ($stackTrace[0]['line'] !== $errLine)
2057:                             )
2058:                     ) {
2059:                         array_unshift( $stackTrace, array(
2060:                                 'line' => $errLine,
2061:                                 'file' => $errFile
2062:                         ) );
2063:                     }
2064: 
2065:                     if ( $stackTrace && !$isEmpty ) {
2066:                         $ignoreCommons = false;
2067:                         $len = count($stackTrace);
2068: 
2069:                         /*
2070:                          * The code above can prioritize a location in the stack trace,
2071:                          * this is 'stackSearchI'. So we should start our search from there,
2072:                          * and work down the stack.
2073:                          * 
2074:                          * This is built in a way so that when it reaches the end, it'll loop
2075:                          * back round to the beginning, and check the traces we didn't check
2076:                          * last time.
2077:                          * 
2078:                          * If stackSearchI was not altered, then it just searches from top
2079:                          * through to the bottom.
2080:                          */
2081:                         for ( $i = $stackSearchI; $i < $stackSearchI+$len; $i++ ) {
2082:                             $trace = &$stackTrace[ $i % $len ];
2083: 
2084:                             if ( isset($trace['file']) && isset($trace['line']) ) {
2085:                                 list( $type, $_ ) = $this->getFolderType( $root, $trace['file'] );
2086: 
2087:                                 if ( $type !== ErrorHandler::FILE_TYPE_IGNORE ) {
2088:                                     if ( $type === ErrorHandler::FILE_TYPE_APPLICATION ) {
2089:                                         $srcErrLine = $trace['line'];
2090:                                         $srcErrFile = $trace['file'];
2091: 
2092:                                         break;
2093:                                     } else if ( ! $ignoreCommons ) {
2094:                                         $srcErrLine = $trace['line'];
2095:                                         $srcErrFile = $trace['file'];
2096: 
2097:                                         $ignoreCommons = true;
2098:                                     }
2099:                                 }
2100:                             }
2101:                         }
2102:                     }
2103:                 }
2104: 
2105:                 return array( $message, $srcErrFile, $srcErrLine, $altInfo );
2106:             }
2107: 
2108:             /**
2109:              * Parses the stack trace, and makes it look pretty.
2110:              * 
2111:              * This includes adding in the syntax highlighting,
2112:              * highlighting the colours for the files,
2113:              * and padding with whitespace.
2114:              *
2115:              * If stackTrace is null, then null is returned.
2116:              */
2117:             private function parseStackTrace( $code, $message, $errLine, $errFile, &$stackTrace, $root, $altInfo=null ) {
2118:                 if ( $stackTrace !== null ) {
2119:                     /*
2120:                      * For whitespace padding.
2121:                      */
2122:                     $lineLen = 0;
2123:                     $fileLen = 0;
2124: 
2125:                     // parse the stack trace, and remove the long urls
2126:                     foreach ( $stackTrace as $i => $trace ) {
2127:                         if ( $trace ) {
2128:                             if ( isset($trace['line'] ) ) {
2129:                                 $lineLen = max( $lineLen, strlen($trace['line']) );
2130:                             } else {
2131:                                 $trace['line'] = '';
2132:                             }
2133: 
2134:                             $info = '';
2135: 
2136:                             if ( $i === 0 && $altInfo !== null ) {
2137:                                 $info = $altInfo;
2138:                             /*
2139:                              * Skip for the first iteration,
2140:                              * as it's usually magical PHP calls.
2141:                              */
2142:                             } else if (
2143:                                 $i > 0 && (
2144:                                         isset($trace['class']) ||
2145:                                         isset($trace['type']) ||
2146:                                         isset($trace['function'])
2147:                                 )
2148:                             ) {
2149:                                 $args = array();
2150:                                 if ( isset($trace['args']) ) {
2151:                                     foreach ( $trace['args'] as $arg ) {
2152:                                         $args[]= ErrorHandler::identifyTypeHTML( $arg, 1 );
2153:                                     }
2154:                                 }
2155: 
2156:                                 $info = ErrorHandler::syntaxHighlightFunction(
2157:                                         isset($trace['class'])      ? $trace['class']       : null,
2158:                                         isset($trace['type'])       ? $trace['type']        : null,
2159:                                         isset($trace['function'])   ? $trace['function']    : null,
2160:                                         $args
2161:                                 );
2162:                             } else if ( isset($trace['info']) && $trace['info'] !== '' ) {
2163:                                 $info = ErrorHandler::syntaxHighlight( $trace['info'] );
2164:                             } else if ( isset($trace['file']) && !isset($trace['info']) ) {
2165:                                 $contents = $this->getFileContents( $trace['file'] );
2166: 
2167:                                 if ( $contents ) {
2168:                                     $info = ErrorHandler::syntaxHighlight(
2169:                                             trim( $contents[$trace['line']-1] )
2170:                                     );
2171:                                 }
2172:                             } 
2173: 
2174:                             $trace['info'] = $info;
2175: 
2176:                             if ( isset($trace['file']) ) {
2177:                                 list( $type, $file ) = $this->getFolderType( $root, $trace['file'] );
2178: 
2179:                                 $trace['file_type'] = $type;
2180:                                 $trace['is_native'] = false;
2181:                             } else {
2182:                                 $file = '[Internal PHP]';
2183: 
2184:                                 $trace['file_type'] = '';
2185:                                 $trace['is_native'] = true;
2186:                             }
2187: 
2188:                             $trace['file'] = $file;
2189: 
2190:                             $fileLen = max( $fileLen, strlen($file) );
2191: 
2192:                             $stackTrace[$i] = $trace;
2193:                         }
2194:                     }
2195: 
2196:                     /*
2197:                      * We are allowed to highlight just once, that's it.
2198:                      */
2199:                     $highlightI = -1;
2200:                     foreach ( $stackTrace as $i => $trace ) {
2201:                         if (
2202:                                 $trace['line'] === $errLine &&
2203:                                 $trace['file'] === $errFile
2204:                         ) {
2205:                             $highlightI = $i;
2206:                             break;
2207:                         }
2208:                     }
2209: 
2210:                     foreach ( $stackTrace as $i => $trace ) {
2211:                         if ( $trace ) {
2212:                             // line
2213:                             $line = str_pad( $trace['line']     , $lineLen, ' ', STR_PAD_LEFT  );
2214: 
2215:                             // file
2216:                             $file = $trace['file'];
2217:                             $fileKlass = '';
2218:                             if ( $trace['is_native'] ) {
2219:                                 $fileKlass = 'file-internal-php';
2220:                             } else {
2221:                                 $fileKlass = 'filename ' . ErrorHandler::folderTypeToCSS( $trace['file_type'] );
2222:                             }
2223:                             $file = $file . str_pad( '', $fileLen-strlen($file), ' ', STR_PAD_LEFT );
2224: 
2225:                             // info
2226:                             $info = $trace['info'];
2227:                             if ( $info ) {
2228:                                 $info = str_replace( "\n", '\n', $info );
2229:                                 $info = str_replace( "\r", '\r', $info );
2230:                             } else {
2231:                                 $info = '&nbsp;';
2232:                             }
2233: 
2234:                             // line + file + info
2235:                             $stackStr =
2236:                                     "<td class='linenumber'>$line</td>" .
2237:                                     "<td class='$fileKlass'>$file</td>" .
2238:                                     "<td class='lineinfo'>$info</td>"   ;
2239: 
2240:                             if ( $trace['is_native'] ) {
2241:                                 $cssClass = 'is-native ';
2242:                             } else {
2243:                                 $cssClass = '';
2244:                             }
2245: 
2246:                             if ( $highlightI === $i ) {
2247:                                 $cssClass .= ' highlight';
2248:                             } else if ( $highlightI > $i ) {
2249:                                 $cssClass .= ' pre-highlight';
2250:                             }
2251: 
2252:                             if (
2253:                                     $i !== 0 &&
2254:                                     isset($trace['exception']) &&
2255:                                     $trace['exception']
2256:                             ) {
2257:                                 $ex = $trace['exception'];
2258: 
2259:                                 $exHtml = '<tr class="error-stack-trace-exception"><td>' .
2260:                                             'exception &quot;' .
2261:                                             htmlspecialchars( $ex->getMessage() ) .
2262:                                             '&quot;' .
2263:                                         '</td></tr>';
2264:                             } else {
2265:                                 $exHtml = '';
2266:                             }
2267: 
2268:                             $data = '';
2269:                             if ( isset($trace['file-lines-id']) ) {
2270:                                 $data = 'data-file-lines-id="' . $trace['file-lines-id'] . '"';
2271:                             }
2272: 
2273:                             $stackTrace[$i] = "$exHtml<tr class='error-stack-trace-line $cssClass' $data>$stackStr</tr>";
2274:                         }
2275:                     }
2276: 
2277:                     return '<table id="error-stack-trace">' . join( "", $stackTrace ) . '</table>';
2278:                 } else {
2279:                     return null;
2280:                 }
2281:             }
2282: 
2283:             private function logError( $message, $file, $line, $ex=null ) {
2284:                 if ( $ex ) {
2285:                     $trace = $ex->getTraceAsString();
2286:                     $parts = explode( "\n", $trace );
2287:                     $trace = "        " . join( "\n        ", $parts );
2288: 
2289:                     if ( ! ErrorHandler::isIIS() ) {
2290:                         error_log( "$message \n           $file, $line \n$trace" );
2291:                     }
2292:                 } else {
2293:                     if ( ! ErrorHandler::isIIS() ) {
2294:                         error_log( "$message \n           $file, $line" );
2295:                     }
2296:                 }
2297:             }
2298: 
2299:             /**
2300:              * Given a class name, which can include a namespace,
2301:              * this will report that it is not found.
2302:              * 
2303:              * This will also report it as an exception,
2304:              * so you will get a full stack trace.
2305:              */
2306:             public function reportClassNotFound( $className ) {
2307:                 throw new ErrorException( "Class '$className' not found", E_ERROR, E_ERROR, __FILE__, __LINE__ );
2308:             }
2309: 
2310:             /**
2311:              * Given an exception, this will report it.
2312:              */
2313:             public function reportException( $ex ) {
2314:                 $this->reportError(
2315:                         $ex->getCode(),
2316:                         $ex->getMessage(),
2317:                         $ex->getLine(),
2318:                         $ex->getFile(),
2319:                         $ex
2320:                 );
2321:             }
2322: 
2323:             /**
2324:              * The entry point for handling an error.
2325:              * 
2326:              * This is the lowest entry point for error reporting,
2327:              * and for that reason it can either take just error info,
2328:              * or a combination of error and exception information.
2329:              * 
2330:              * Note that this will still log errors in the error log
2331:              * even when it's disabled with ini. It just does nothing
2332:              * more than that.
2333:              */
2334:             public function reportError( $code, $message, $errLine, $errFile, $ex=null ) {
2335:                 $this->discardBuffer();
2336: 
2337:                 if (
2338:                         $ex === null &&
2339:                         $code === 1 &&
2340:                         strpos($message, "Class ") === 0 &&
2341:                         strpos($message, "not found") !== false &&
2342:                         $this->classNotFoundException !== null
2343:                 ) {
2344:                     $ex = $this->classNotFoundException;
2345: 
2346:                     $code       = $ex->getCode();
2347:                     $message    = $ex->getMessage();
2348:                     $errLine    = $ex->getLine();
2349:                     $errFile    = $ex->getFile();
2350:                     $stackTrace = $ex->getTrace();
2351:                 }
2352: 
2353:                 $this->logError( $message, $errFile, $errLine, $ex );
2354: 
2355:                 /**
2356:                  * It runs if:
2357:                  *  - it is globally enabled
2358:                  *  - this error handler is enabled
2359:                  *  - we believe it is a regular html request, or ajax
2360:                  */
2361:                 global $_php_error_is_ini_enabled;
2362:                 if (
2363:                         $_php_error_is_ini_enabled &&
2364:                         $this->isOn() && (
2365:                                 $this->isAjax ||
2366:                                 !$this->htmlOnly ||
2367:                                 !ErrorHandler::isNonPHPRequest()
2368:                         )
2369:                 ) {
2370:                     $root = $this->applicationRoot;
2371: 
2372:                     list( $ex, $stackTrace, $code, $errFile, $errLine ) =
2373:                             $this->getStackTrace( $ex, $code, $errFile, $errLine );
2374: 
2375:                     list( $message, $srcErrFile, $srcErrLine, $altInfo ) =
2376:                             $this->improveErrorMessage(
2377:                                     $ex,
2378:                                     $code,
2379:                                     $message,
2380:                                     $errLine,
2381:                                     $errFile,
2382:                                     $root,
2383:                                     $stackTrace
2384:                             );
2385: 
2386:                     $errFile = $srcErrFile;
2387:                     $errLine = $srcErrLine;
2388: 
2389:                     list( $fileLinesSets, $numFileLines ) = $this->generateFileLineSets( $srcErrFile, $srcErrLine, $stackTrace );
2390: 
2391:                     list( $type, $errFile ) = $this->getFolderType( $root, $errFile );
2392:                     $errFileType = ErrorHandler::folderTypeToCSS( $type );
2393: 
2394:                     $stackTrace = $this->parseStackTrace( $code, $message, $errLine, $errFile, $stackTrace, $root, $altInfo );
2395:                     $fileLines  = $this->readCodeFile( $srcErrFile, $srcErrLine );
2396: 
2397:                     // load the session, if it's there
2398: 
2399:                     if ( isset($_COOKIE[session_name()]) && session_id() !== '' ) {
2400:                         session_start();
2401:                     }
2402: 
2403:                     $request  = ErrorHandler::getRequestHeaders();
2404:                     $response = ErrorHandler::getResponseHeaders();
2405: 
2406:                     $dump = $this->generateDumpHTML(
2407:                             array(
2408:                                     'post'    => ( isset($_POST)    ? $_POST    : array() ),
2409:                                     'get'     => ( isset($_GET)     ? $_GET     : array() ),
2410:                                     'session' => ( isset($_SESSION) ? $_SESSION : array() ),
2411:                                     'cookies' => ( isset($_COOKIE)  ? $_COOKIE  : array() )
2412:                             ),
2413: 
2414:                             $request,
2415:                             $response,
2416: 
2417:                             $_SERVER
2418:                     );
2419:                     $this->displayError( $message, $srcErrLine, $errFile, $errFileType, $stackTrace, $fileLinesSets, $numFileLines, $dump );
2420: 
2421:                     // exit in order to end processing
2422:                     $this->turnOff();
2423:                     exit(0);
2424:                 }
2425:             }
2426: 
2427:             private function getStackTrace( $ex, $code, $errFile, $errLine ) {
2428:                 $stackTrace = null;
2429: 
2430:                 if ( $ex !== null ) {
2431:                     $next = $ex;
2432:                     $stackTrace = array();
2433:                     $skipStacks = 0;
2434: 
2435:                     for (
2436:                             $next = $ex;
2437:                             $next !== null;
2438:                             $next = $next->getPrevious()
2439:                     ) {
2440:                         $ex = $next;
2441: 
2442:                         $stack = $ex->getTrace();
2443:                         $file  = $ex->getFile();
2444:                         $line  = $ex->getLine();
2445: 
2446:                         if ( $stackTrace !== null && count($stackTrace) > 0 ) {
2447:                             $stack = array_slice( $stack, 0, count($stack)-count($stackTrace) + 1 );
2448:                         }
2449: 
2450:                         if ( count($stack) > 0 && (
2451:                             !isset($stack[0]['file']) ||
2452:                             !isset($stack[0]['line']) ||
2453:                             $stack[0]['file'] !== $file ||
2454:                             $stack[0]['line'] !== $line
2455:                         ) ) {
2456:                             array_unshift( $stack, array(
2457:                                     'file' => $file,
2458:                                     'line' => $line
2459:                             ) );
2460:                         }
2461: 
2462:                         $stackTrace = ( $stackTrace !== null ) ?
2463:                                 array_merge( $stack, $stackTrace ) :
2464:                                 $stack ;
2465: 
2466:                         if ( count($stackTrace) > 0 ) {
2467:                             $stackTrace[0]['exception'] = $ex;
2468:                         }
2469:                     }
2470: 
2471:                     $message = $ex->getMessage();
2472:                     $errFile = $ex->getFile();
2473:                     $errLine = $ex->getLine();
2474: 
2475:                     $code = method_exists($ex, 'getSeverity') ?
2476:                             $ex->getSeverity() :
2477:                             $ex->getCode()     ;
2478:                 }
2479: 
2480:                 return array( $ex, $stackTrace, $code, $errFile, $errLine );
2481:             }
2482: 
2483:             private function generateDumpHTML( $arrays, $request, $response, $server ) {
2484:                 $arrToHtml = function( $name, $array, $css='' ) {
2485:                     $max = 0;
2486: 
2487:                     foreach ( $array as $e => $v ) {
2488:                         $max = max( $max, strlen( $e ) );
2489:                     }
2490: 
2491:                     $snippet = "<h2 class='error_dump_header'>$name</h2>";
2492: 
2493:                     foreach ( $array as $e => $v ) {
2494:                         $e = str_pad( $e, $max, ' ', STR_PAD_RIGHT );
2495: 
2496:                         $e = htmlentities( $e );
2497:                         $v = ErrorHandler::identifyTypeHTML( $v, 3 );
2498: 
2499:                         $snippet .= "<div class='error_dump_key'>$e</div><div class='error_dump_mapping'>=&gt;</div><div class='error_dump_value'>$v</div>";
2500:                     }
2501: 
2502:                     return "<div class='error_dump $css'>$snippet</div>";
2503:                 };
2504: 
2505:                 $html = '';
2506:                 foreach ( $arrays as $key => $value ) {
2507:                     if ( isset($value) && $value ) {
2508:                         $html .= $arrToHtml( $key, $value );
2509:                     } else {
2510:                         unset($arrays[$key]);
2511:                     }
2512:                 }
2513: 
2514:                 return "<div class='error-dumps'>" .
2515:                             $html .
2516:                             $arrToHtml( 'request', $request, 'dump_request' ) .
2517:                             $arrToHtml( 'response', $response, 'dump_response' ) .
2518:                             $arrToHtml( 'server', $server, 'dump_server' ) .
2519:                         "</div>";
2520:             }
2521: 
2522:             private function generateFileLineSets( $srcErrFile, $srcErrLine, &$stackTrace ) {
2523:                 $fileLineID = 1;
2524:                 $srcErrID = "file-line-$fileLineID";
2525:                 $fileLineID++;
2526: 
2527:                 $lines = $this->readCodeFile( $srcErrFile, $srcErrLine );
2528:                 $minSize = count( $lines );
2529:                 $fileLinesSets = array( new FileLinesSet( $srcErrLine, $srcErrID, $lines, true ) );
2530: 
2531:                 if ( $stackTrace ) {
2532:                     foreach ( $stackTrace as $i => &$trace ) {
2533:                         if ( $trace && isset($trace['file']) && isset($trace['line']) ) {
2534:                             $file = $trace['file'];
2535:                             $line = $trace['line'];
2536: 
2537:                             if ( $file === $srcErrFile && $line === $srcErrLine ) {
2538:                                 $trace['file-lines-id'] = $srcErrID;
2539:                             } else {
2540:                                 $traceFileID = "file-line-$fileLineID";
2541:                                 $trace['file-lines-id'] = $traceFileID;
2542: 
2543:                                 $lines = $this->readCodeFile( $file, $line );
2544:                                 $minSize = max( $minSize, count($lines) );
2545:                                 $fileLinesSets[]= new FileLinesSet( $line, $traceFileID, $lines, false );
2546: 
2547:                                 $fileLineID++;
2548:                             }
2549:                         }
2550:                     }
2551:                 }
2552: 
2553:                 return array( $fileLinesSets, $minSize );
2554:             }
2555: 
2556:             /*
2557:              * Even if disabled, we still act like reporting is on,
2558:              * if it's turned on.
2559:              * 
2560:              * We just don't do anything.
2561:              */
2562:             private function setEnabled( $isOn ) {
2563:                 $wasOn = $this->isOn;
2564:                 $this->isOn = $isOn;
2565: 
2566:                 global $_php_error_is_ini_enabled;
2567:                 if ( $_php_error_is_ini_enabled ) {
2568:                     /*
2569:                      * Only turn off, if we're moving from on to off.
2570:                      * 
2571:                      * This is so if it's turned off without turning on,
2572:                      * we don't change anything.
2573:                      */
2574:                     if ( !$isOn ) {
2575:                         if ( $wasOn ) {
2576:                             $this->runDisableErrors();
2577:                         }
2578:                     /*
2579:                      * Always turn it on, even if already on.
2580:                      * 
2581:                      * This is incase it was messed up in some way
2582:                      * by the user.
2583:                      */
2584:                     } else if ( $isOn ) {
2585:                         $this->runEnableErrors();
2586:                     }
2587:                 }
2588:             }
2589: 
2590:             private function runDisableErrors() {
2591:                 global $_php_error_is_ini_enabled;
2592: 
2593:                 if ( $_php_error_is_ini_enabled ) {
2594:                     error_reporting( $this->defaultErrorReportingOff );
2595: 
2596:                     @ini_restore( 'html_errors' );
2597:                     
2598:                     if ( ErrorHandler::isIIS() ) {
2599:                         @ini_restore( 'log_errors' );
2600:                     }
2601:                 }
2602:             }
2603: 
2604:             /*
2605:              * Now the actual hooking into PHP's error reporting.
2606:              * 
2607:              * We enable _ALL_ errors, and make them all exceptions.
2608:              * We also need to hook into the shutdown function so
2609:              * we can catch fatal and compile time errors.
2610:              */
2611:             private function runEnableErrors() {
2612:                 global $_php_error_is_ini_enabled;
2613:                 
2614:                 if ( $_php_error_is_ini_enabled ) {
2615:                     $catchSurpressedErrors = &$this->catchSurpressedErrors;
2616:                     $self = $this;
2617: 
2618:                     // all errors \o/ !
2619:                     error_reporting( $this->defaultErrorReportingOn );
2620:                     @ini_set( 'html_errors', false );
2621: 
2622:                     if ( ErrorHandler::isIIS() ) {
2623:                         @ini_set( 'log_errors', false );
2624:                     }
2625: 
2626:                     set_error_handler(
2627:                             function( $code, $message, $file, $line, $context ) use ( $self, &$catchSurpressedErrors ) {
2628:                                 /*
2629:                                  * DO NOT! log the error.
2630:                                  * 
2631:                                  * Either it's thrown as an exception, and so logged by the exception handler,
2632:                                  * or we return false, and it's logged by PHP.
2633:                                  * 
2634:                                  * Also DO NOT! throw an exception, instead report it.
2635:                                  * This is because if an operation raises both a user AND
2636:                                  * fatal error (such as require), then the exception is
2637:                                  * silently ignored.
2638:                                  */
2639:                                 if ( $self->isOn() ) {
2640:                                     /*
2641:                                      * When using an @, the error reporting drops to 0.
2642:                                      */
2643:                                     if ( error_reporting() !== 0 || $catchSurpressedErrors ) {
2644:                                         $ex = new ErrorException( $message, $code, $code, $file, $line );
2645: 
2646:                                         $self->reportException( $ex );
2647:                                     }
2648:                                 } else {
2649:                                     return false;
2650:                                 }
2651:                             },
2652:                             $this->defaultErrorReportingOn 
2653:                     );
2654: 
2655:                     set_exception_handler( function($ex) use ( $self ) {
2656:                         if ( $self->isOn() ) {
2657:                             $self->reportException( $ex );
2658:                         } else {
2659:                             return false;
2660:                         }
2661:                     });
2662: 
2663:                     if ( ! $self->isShutdownRegistered ) {
2664:                         if ( $self->catchClassNotFound ) {
2665:                             $classException = &$self->classNotFoundException;
2666:                             $autoloaderFuns = ErrorHandler::$SAFE_AUTOLOADER_FUNCTIONS;
2667: 
2668:                             /*
2669:                              * When this is called, the key point is that we don't error!
2670:                              *
2671:                              * Instead we record that an error has occurred,
2672:                              * if we believe one has, and then let PHP error as normal.
2673:                              * The stack trace we record is then used later.
2674:                              *
2675:                              * This is done for two reasons:
2676:                              *  - functions like 'class_exists' will run the autoloader, and we shouldn't error on them
2677:                              *  - on PHP 5.3.0, the class loader registered functions does *not* return closure objects, so we can't do anything clever.
2678:                              * 
2679:                              * So we watch, but don't touch.
2680:                              */
2681:                             spl_autoload_register( function($className) use ( $self, &$classException, &$autoloaderFuns ) {
2682:                                 if ( $self->isOn() ) {
2683:                                     $classException = null;
2684: 
2685:                                     // search the stack first, to check if we are running from 'class_exists' before we error
2686:                                     if ( defined('DEBUG_BACKTRACE_IGNORE_ARGS') ) {
2687:                                         $trace = debug_backtrace( DEBUG_BACKTRACE_IGNORE_ARGS );
2688:                                     } else {
2689:                                         $trace = debug_backtrace();
2690:                                     }
2691:                                     $error = true;
2692: 
2693:                                     foreach ( $trace as $row ) {
2694:                                         if ( isset($row['function']) ) {
2695:                                             $function = $row['function'];
2696: 
2697:                                             // they are just checking, so don't error
2698:                                             if ( in_array($function, $autoloaderFuns, true) ) {
2699:                                                 $error = false;
2700:                                                 break;
2701:                                             // not us, and not the autoloader, so error!
2702:                                             } else if (
2703:                                                     $function !== '__autoload' &&
2704:                                                     $function !== 'spl_autoload_call' &&
2705:                                                     strpos($function, 'php_error\\') === false
2706:                                             ) {
2707:                                                 break;
2708:                                             }
2709:                                         }
2710:                                     }
2711: 
2712:                                     if ( $error ) {
2713:                                         $classException = new ErrorException( "Class '$className' not found", E_ERROR, E_ERROR, __FILE__, __LINE__ );
2714:                                     }
2715:                                 }
2716:                             } );
2717:                         }
2718: 
2719:                         $self->isShutdownRegistered = true;
2720:                     }
2721:                 }
2722:             }
2723: 
2724:             private function displayJSInjection() {
2725:                 ?><script data-php_error="magic JS, just ignore this!">
2726:                     "use strict";
2727: 
2728:                     (function( window ) {
2729:                         if ( window.XMLHttpRequest ) {
2730:                             /** 
2731:                              * A method wrapping helper function.
2732:                              * 
2733:                              * Wraps the method given, from the old prototype to the new
2734:                              * XMLHttpRequest prototype.
2735:                              * 
2736:                              * This only happens if the old one actually has that prototype.
2737:                              * If the browser doesn't support a prototype, then it doesn't
2738:                              * get wrapped.
2739:                              */
2740:                             var wrapMethod = function( XMLHttpRequest, old, prop ) {
2741:                                 if ( old.prototype[prop] ) {
2742:                                     var behaviours = ( arguments.length > 3 ) ?
2743:                                             Array.prototype.slice.call( arguments, 3 ) :
2744:                                             null ;
2745: 
2746:                                     XMLHttpRequest.prototype[prop] = function() {
2747:                                         if ( behaviours !== null ) {
2748:                                             for ( var i = 0; i < behaviours.length; i++ ) {
2749:                                                 behaviours[i].call( this, arguments, prop );
2750:                                             }
2751:                                         }
2752: 
2753:                                         return this.__.inner[prop].apply( this.__.inner, arguments );
2754:                                     };
2755:                                 }
2756:                             }
2757: 
2758:                             var postMethod = function( XMLHttpRequest, prop ) {
2759:                                 if ( XMLHttpRequest.prototype[prop] ) {
2760:                                     var behaviours = Array.prototype.slice.call( arguments, 2 );
2761: 
2762:                                     var previous = XMLHttpRequest.prototype[prop];
2763:                                     XMLHttpRequest.prototype[prop] = function() {
2764:                                         var r = previous.apply( this, arguments );
2765: 
2766:                                         for ( var i = 0; i < behaviours.length; i++ ) {
2767:                                             behaviours[i].call( this, arguments, prop );
2768:                                         }
2769: 
2770:                                         return r;
2771:                                     };
2772:                                 }
2773:                             }
2774: 
2775:                             /*
2776:                              * Certain properties will error when read,
2777:                              * and which ones do vary from browser to browser.
2778:                              * 
2779:                              * I've found both Chrome and Firefox will error
2780:                              * on _different_ properties.
2781:                              * 
2782:                              * So every read needs to be wrapped in a try/catch,
2783:                              * and just hope it doesn't error.
2784:                              */
2785:                             var copyProperties = function( src, dest, props ) {
2786:                                 for ( var i = 0; i < props.length; i++ ) {
2787:                                     try {
2788:                                         var prop = props[i];
2789:                                         dest[prop] = src[prop];
2790:                                     } catch( ex ) { }
2791:                                 }
2792:                             };
2793: 
2794:                             var copyResponseProperties = function( src, dest ) {
2795:                                 copyProperties( src, dest, [
2796:                                         'response',
2797:                                         'responseText',
2798:                                         'responseXML'
2799:                                 ]);
2800:                             }
2801: 
2802:                             var copyRequestProperties = function( src, dest, includeReadOnly, skipResponse ) {
2803:                                 copyProperties( src, dest, [
2804:                                         'readyState',
2805:                                         'timeout',
2806:                                         'upload',
2807:                                         'withCredentials',
2808:                                         'responseType',
2809: 
2810:                                         'mozBackgroundRequest',
2811:                                         'mozArrayBuffer',
2812:                                         'multipart'
2813:                                 ]);
2814: 
2815:                                 if ( includeReadOnly ) {
2816:                                     copyProperties( src, dest, [
2817:                                             'status',
2818:                                             'statusText',
2819:                                             'channel'
2820:                                     ]);
2821: 
2822:                                     if ( ! skipResponse ) {
2823:                                         copyResponseProperties( src, dest );
2824:                                     }
2825:                                 }
2826: 
2827:                                 return dest;
2828:                             }
2829: 
2830:                             var runFail = function( ev ) {
2831:                                 var self = this;
2832:                                 var xmlHttpRequest = this.__.inner;
2833: 
2834:                                 var iframe = document.createElement('iframe');
2835:                                 iframe.setAttribute('width', '100%');
2836:                                 iframe.setAttribute('height', '100%');
2837:                                 iframe.setAttribute('src', 'about:blank');
2838: 
2839:                                 iframe.style.transition =
2840:                                 iframe.style.OTransition =
2841:                                 iframe.style.MsTransition =
2842:                                 iframe.style.MozTransition =
2843:                                 iframe.style.WebkitTransition = 'opacity 200ms linear';
2844: 
2845:                                 iframe.style.background = 'transparent';
2846:                                 iframe.style.opacity = 0;
2847:                                 iframe.style.zIndex = 100001;
2848:                                 iframe.style.top = 0;
2849:                                 iframe.style.right = 0;
2850:                                 iframe.style.left = 0;
2851:                                 iframe.style.bottom = 0;
2852:                                 iframe.style.position = 'fixed';
2853: 
2854:                                 var response = xmlHttpRequest.responseText;
2855: 
2856:                                 iframe.onload = function() {
2857:                                     var iDoc = iframe.contentWindow || iframe.contentDocument;
2858:                                     if ( iDoc.document) {
2859:                                         iDoc = iDoc.document;
2860:                                     }
2861: 
2862:                                     var iBody = iDoc.getElementsByTagName("body")[0];
2863:                                     iBody.innerHTML = response; 
2864:                                     var iHead = iDoc.getElementsByTagName("head")[0];
2865: 
2866:                                     // re-run the script tags
2867:                                     var scripts = iDoc.getElementsByTagName('script');
2868:                                     for ( var i = 0; i < scripts.length; i++ ) {
2869:                                         var script = scripts[i];
2870:                                         var parent = script.parentNode;
2871: 
2872:                                         if ( parent ) {
2873:                                             parent.removeChild( script );
2874: 
2875:                                             var newScript = iDoc.createElement('script');
2876:                                             newScript.innerHTML = script.innerHTML;
2877: 
2878:                                             iHead.appendChild( newScript );
2879:                                         }
2880:                                     }
2881: 
2882:                                     var closed = false;
2883:                                     var closeIFrame = function() {
2884:                                         if ( ! closed ) {
2885:                                             closed = true;
2886: 
2887:                                             iframe.style.opacity = 0;
2888: 
2889:                                             setTimeout( function() {
2890:                                                 iframe.parentNode.removeChild( iframe );
2891:                                             }, 220 );
2892:                                         }
2893:                                     }
2894: 
2895:                                     /*
2896:                                      * Retry Handler.
2897:                                      * 
2898:                                      * Clear this, make a new (real) XMLHttpRequest,
2899:                                      * and then re-run everything.
2900:                                      */
2901:                                     iDoc.getElementById('ajax-retry').onclick = function() {
2902:                                         var methodCalls = self.__.methodCalls;
2903: 
2904:                                         initializeXMLHttpRequest.call( self );
2905:                                         for ( var i = 0; i < methodCalls.length; i++ ) {
2906:                                             var method = methodCalls[i];
2907:                                             self[method.method].apply( self, method.args );
2908:                                         }
2909: 
2910:                                         closeIFrame();
2911: 
2912:                                         return false;
2913:                                     };
2914: 
2915:                                     /*
2916:                                      * The close handler.
2917:                                      * 
2918:                                      * When closed, the response is cleared,
2919:                                      * and then the request finishes with null info.
2920:                                      */
2921:                                     iDoc.getElementById('ajax-close').onclick = function() {
2922:                                         copyRequestProperties( self.__.inner, self, true );
2923: 
2924:                                         // clear the response
2925:                                         self.response       = '';
2926:                                         self.responseText   = '';
2927:                                         self.responseXML    = null;
2928: 
2929:                                         if ( self.onreadystatechange ) {
2930:                                             self.onreadystatechange( ev );
2931:                                         }
2932: 
2933:                                         closeIFrame();
2934:                                         return false;
2935:                                     };
2936: 
2937:                                     var html = iDoc.getElementsByTagName('html')[0];
2938:                                     html.setAttribute( 'class', 'ajax' );
2939: 
2940:                                     setTimeout( function() {
2941:                                         iframe.style.opacity = 1;
2942:                                     }, 1 );
2943:                                 }
2944: 
2945:                                 /*
2946:                                  * Placed inside a timeout, incase the document doesn't exist yet.
2947:                                  * 
2948:                                  * Can happen if the page ajax's straight away.
2949:                                  */
2950:                                 setTimeout( function() {
2951:                                     var body = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0];
2952:                                     body.appendChild( iframe );
2953:                                 }, 1 );
2954:                             }
2955: 
2956:                             var old = window.XMLHttpRequest;
2957: 
2958:                             /**
2959:                              * The middle man http request object.
2960:                              * 
2961:                              * Acts just like a normal one, but will show errors if they
2962:                              * occur instead of running the result.
2963:                              */
2964:                             var XMLHttpRequest = function() {
2965:                                 initializeXMLHttpRequest.call( this );
2966:                             }
2967: 
2968:                             var initializeXMLHttpRequest = function() {
2969:                                 var self = this,
2970:                                     inner = new old();
2971: 
2972:                                 /**
2973:                                  * With a buggy XMLHttpRequest, it's possible to accidentally run the error handler
2974:                                  * multiple times.
2975:                                  * 
2976:                                  * This is a flag to only do it once, to keep the code more defensive.
2977:                                  */
2978:                                 var errorOnce   = true,
2979:                                     isAjaxError = false;
2980: 
2981:                                 var stateResults = [];
2982: 
2983:                                 inner.onreadystatechange = function( ev ) {
2984:                                     copyRequestProperties( inner, self, true, true );
2985: 
2986:                                     var state = inner.readyState;
2987: 
2988:                                     /*
2989:                                      * Check headers for error.
2990:                                      */
2991:                                     if ( ! isAjaxError && state >= 2 ) {
2992:                                         var header = inner.getResponseHeader( '<?php echo ErrorHandler::PHP_ERROR_MAGIC_HEADER_KEY ?>' );
2993: 
2994:                                         if ( header !== null ) {
2995:                                             self.__.isAjaxError = true;
2996:                                             isAjaxError = true;
2997:                                         }
2998:                                     }
2999: 
3000:                                     if ( ! isAjaxError && state >= 2 ) {
3001:                                         copyResponseProperties( inner, self );
3002:                                     }
3003: 
3004:                                     /*
3005:                                      * Success ! \o/
3006:                                      * 
3007:                                      * Pass any state change on to the parent caller,
3008:                                      * unless we hit an ajaxy error.
3009:                                      */
3010:                                     if ( !isAjaxError && self.onreadystatechange ) {
3011:                                         /*
3012:                                          * One of three things happens:
3013:                                          *  = cache the requests until we know there is no error (state 4)
3014:                                          *  = we know there is no error, and so we run our cache
3015:                                          *  = cache is done, but we've been called again, so just pass it on
3016:                                          */
3017:                                         if ( state < 4 ) {
3018:                                             stateResults.push( copyRequestProperties(self, {}, true) );
3019:                                         } else {
3020:                                             if ( stateResults !== null ) {
3021:                                                 var currentState = copyRequestProperties( self, {}, true );
3022: 
3023:                                                 for ( var i = 0; i < stateResults.length; i++ ) {
3024:                                                     var store = stateResults[i];
3025:                                                     copyRequestProperties( store, self, true );
3026: 
3027:                                                     // must check a second time here,
3028:                                                     // in case it gets changed within an onreadystatechange
3029:                                                     if ( self.onreadystatechange ) {
3030:                                                         self.onreadystatechange( ev );
3031:                                                     }
3032:                                                 }
3033: 
3034:                                                 copyRequestProperties( currentState, self, true );
3035:                                                 stateResults = null;
3036:                                             }
3037: 
3038:                                             if ( self.onreadystatechange ) {
3039:                                                 self.onreadystatechange( ev );
3040:                                             }
3041:                                         }
3042:                                     }
3043: 
3044:                                     /*
3045:                                      * Fail : (
3046:                                      */
3047:                                     if (
3048:                                             isAjaxError &&
3049:                                             state === 4 &&
3050:                                             errorOnce
3051:                                     ) {
3052:                                         errorOnce = false;
3053:                                         runFail.call( self, ev );
3054:                                     }
3055:                                 };
3056: 
3057:                                 copyRequestProperties( inner, this, true );
3058: 
3059:                                 /*
3060:                                  * Private fields are stored underneath an unhappy face,
3061:                                  * to localize them.
3062:                                  * 
3063:                                  * Access becomes:
3064:                                  *  this.__.fieldName
3065:                                  */
3066:                                 this.__ = {
3067:                                         methodCalls: [],
3068:                                         inner: inner,
3069:                                         isAjaxError: false,
3070:                                         isSynchronous: false
3071:                                 };
3072:                             }
3073: 
3074:                             /*
3075:                              * We build the methods for the fake XMLHttpRequest.
3076:                              */
3077: 
3078:                             var copyIn = function() {
3079:                                 copyRequestProperties( this, this.__.inner );
3080:                             }
3081:                             var copyOut = function() {
3082:                                 copyRequestProperties( this.__.inner, this, true, this.__.isSynchronous && this.__.isAjaxError );
3083:                             }
3084:                             var addHeader = function() {
3085:                                 this.__.inner.setRequestHeader( 'HTTP_X_REQUESTED_WITH', 'XMLHttpRequest' );
3086:                             }
3087:                             var isSynchronous = function( args ) {
3088:                                 this.__.isSynchronous = ( args[2] === false );
3089:                             }
3090:                             var saveRequest = function( args, method ) {
3091:                                 this.__.methodCalls.push({
3092:                                     method: method,
3093:                                     args: args
3094:                                 });
3095:                             }
3096: 
3097:                             wrapMethod( XMLHttpRequest, old, 'open'        , saveRequest, copyIn, isSynchronous );
3098:                             wrapMethod( XMLHttpRequest, old, 'abort'       , saveRequest, copyIn );
3099:                             wrapMethod( XMLHttpRequest, old, 'send'        , saveRequest, copyIn, addHeader );
3100:                             wrapMethod( XMLHttpRequest, old, 'sendAsBinary', saveRequest, copyIn, addHeader );
3101: 
3102:                             postMethod( XMLHttpRequest,      'send'        , copyOut );
3103:                             postMethod( XMLHttpRequest,      'sendAsBinary', copyOut );
3104: 
3105:                             wrapMethod( XMLHttpRequest, old, 'getAllResponseHeaders', saveRequest );
3106:                             wrapMethod( XMLHttpRequest, old, 'getResponseHeader'    , saveRequest );
3107:                             wrapMethod( XMLHttpRequest, old, 'setRequestHeader'     , saveRequest );
3108:                             wrapMethod( XMLHttpRequest, old, 'overrideMimeType'     , saveRequest );
3109: 
3110:                             window.XMLHttpRequest = XMLHttpRequest;
3111:                         }
3112:                     })( window );
3113:                 </script><?php
3114:             }

3119:              */
3120:             private function displayError( $message, $errLine, $errFile, $errFileType, $stackTrace, &$fileLinesSets, $numFileLines, $dumpInfo ) {
3121:                 $applicationRoot   = $this->applicationRoot;

3137:                         $requestUrl = substr( $requestUrl, 0, $requestUrlLen-1 );

3307:             /**
3308:              * A generic function for clearing the buffer, and displaying error output.
3309:              * 
3310:              * A function needs to be given, and then this is run at the correct time.
3311:              * There are two ways this can be used:
3312:              * 
3313:              *  displayHTML( $head, $body )
3314:              * 
3315:              * Here 'head' is run straight after the doctype, whilst 'body' is run as
3316:              * the body for the content. The other way is:
3317:              * 
3318:              *  displayHTML( $body )
3319:              * 
3320:              * Here there is only content.
3321:              */

4005:         /**

4007:          *
4008:          * This is pretty much a direct port of jsmin.c to PHP with just a few
4009:          * PHP-specific performance tweaks. Also, whereas jsmin.c reads from stdin and
4010:          * outputs to stdout, this library accepts a string as input and returns another
4011:          * string as output.

4051:         class JSMin
4052:         {
4053:             const ORD_LF = 10;
4054:             const ORD_SPACE = 32;
4055:             const ACTION_KEEP_A = 1;
4056:             const ACTION_DELETE_A = 2;
4057:             const ACTION_DELETE_A_B = 3;
4058: 
4059:             protected $a = '';
4060:             protected $b = '';
4061:             protected $input = '';
4062:             protected $inputIndex = 0;
4063:             protected $inputLength = 0;
4064:             protected $lookAhead = null;
4065:             protected $output = '';
4066: 
4067:             // -- Public Static Methods --------------------------------------------------
4068: 
4069:             /**
4070:              * Minify Javascript
4071:              *
4072:              * @uses __construct()
4073:              * @uses min()
4074:              * @param string $js Javascript to be minified
4075:              * @return string
4076:              */
4077:             public static function minify($js) {
4078:                 $jsmin = new JSMin($js);
4079:                 return $jsmin->min();
4080:             }
4081: 
4082:             // -- Public Instance Methods ------------------------------------------------
4083: 
4084:             /**
4085:              * Constructor
4086:              *
4087:              * @param string $input Javascript to be minified
4088:              */
4089:             public function __construct($input) {
4090:                 $this->input = str_replace("\r\n", "\n", $input);
4091:                 $this->inputLength = strlen($this->input);
4092:             }
4093: 
4094:             // -- Protected Instance Methods ---------------------------------------------
4095: 
4096:             /**
4097:              * Action -- do something! What to do is determined by the $command argument.
4098:              *
4099:              * action treats a string as a single character. Wow!
4100:              * action recognizes a regular expression if it is preceded by ( or , or =.
4101:              *
4102:              * @uses next()
4103:              * @uses get()
4104:              * @throws JSMinException If parser errors are found:
4105:              * - Unterminated string literal
4106:              * - Unterminated regular expression set in regex literal
4107:              * - Unterminated regular expression literal
4108:              * @param int $command One of class constants:
4109:              * ACTION_KEEP_A Output A. Copy B to A. Get the next B.
4110:              * ACTION_DELETE_A Copy B to A. Get the next B. (Delete A).
4111:              * ACTION_DELETE_A_B Get the next B. (Delete B).
4112:              */
4113:             protected function action($command) {
4114:                 switch($command) {
4115:                     case self::ACTION_KEEP_A:
4116:                         $this->output .= $this->a;
4117: 
4118:                     case self::ACTION_DELETE_A:
4119:                         $this->a = $this->b;
4120: 
4121:                         if ($this->a === "'" || $this->a === '"') {
4122:                             for (;;) {
4123:                                 $this->output .= $this->a;
4124:                                 $this->a = $this->get();
4125: 
4126:                                 if ($this->a === $this->b) {
4127:                                     break;
4128:                                 }
4129: 
4130:                                 if (ord($this->a) <= self::ORD_LF) {
4131:                                     throw new JSMinException('Unterminated string literal.');
4132:                                 }
4133: 
4134:                                 if ($this->a === '\\') {
4135:                                     $this->output .= $this->a;
4136:                                     $this->a = $this->get();
4137:                                 }
4138:                             }
4139:                         }
4140: 
4141:                     case self::ACTION_DELETE_A_B:
4142:                         $this->b = $this->next();
4143: 
4144:                         if ($this->b === '/' && (
4145:                                 $this->a === '(' || $this->a === ',' || $this->a === '=' ||
4146:                                 $this->a === ':' || $this->a === '[' || $this->a === '!' ||
4147:                                 $this->a === '&' || $this->a === '|' || $this->a === '?' ||
4148:                                 $this->a === '{' || $this->a === '}' || $this->a === ';' ||
4149:                                 $this->a === "\n" )) {
4150: 
4151:                             $this->output .= $this->a . $this->b;
4152: 
4153:                             for (;;) {
4154:                                 $this->a = $this->get();
4155: 
4156:                                 if ($this->a === '[') {
4157:                                     /*
4158:         inside a regex [...] set, which MAY contain a '/' itself. Example: mootools Form.Validator near line 460:
4159:         return Form.Validator.getValidator('IsEmpty').test(element) || (/^(?:[a-z0-9!#$%&'*+/=?^_`{|}~-]\.?){0,63}[a-z0-9!#$%&'*+/=?^_`{|}~-]@(?:(?:[a-z0-9](?:[a-z0-9-]{0,61}[a-z0-9])?\.)*[a-z0-9](?:[a-z0-9-]{0,61}[a-z0-9])?|\[(?:(?:25[0-5]|2[0-4][0-9]|[01]?[0-9][0-9]?)\.){3}(?:25[0-5]|2[0-4][0-9]|[01]?[0-9][0-9]?)\])$/i).test(element.get('value'));
4160:              */
4161:                                     for (;;) {
4162:                                         $this->output .= $this->a;
4163:                                         $this->a = $this->get();
4164: 
4165:                                         if ($this->a === ']') {
4166:                                                 break;
4167:                                         } elseif ($this->a === '\\') {
4168:                                             $this->output .= $this->a;
4169:                                             $this->a = $this->get();
4170:                                         } elseif (ord($this->a) <= self::ORD_LF) {
4171:                                             throw new JSMinException('Unterminated regular expression set in regex literal.');
4172:                                         }
4173:                                     }
4174:                                 } elseif ($this->a === '/') {
4175:                                     break;
4176:                                 } elseif ($this->a === '\\') {
4177:                                     $this->output .= $this->a;
4178:                                     $this->a = $this->get();
4179:                                 } elseif (ord($this->a) <= self::ORD_LF) {
4180:                                     throw new JSMinException('Unterminated regular expression literal.');
4181:                                 }
4182: 
4183:                                 $this->output .= $this->a;
4184:                             }
4185: 
4186:                             $this->b = $this->next();
4187:                         }
4188:                 }
4189:             }
4190: 
4191:             /**
4192:              * Get next char. Convert ctrl char to space.
4193:              *
4194:              * @return string|null
4195:              */
4196:             protected function get() {
4197:                 $c = $this->lookAhead;
4198:                 $this->lookAhead = null;
4199: 
4200:                 if ($c === null) {
4201:                     if ($this->inputIndex < $this->inputLength) {
4202:                         $c = substr($this->input, $this->inputIndex, 1);
4203:                         $this->inputIndex += 1;
4204:                     } else {
4205:                         $c = null;
4206:                     }
4207:                 }
4208: 
4209:                 if ($c === "\r") {
4210:                     return "\n";
4211:                 }
4212: 
4213:                 if ($c === null || $c === "\n" || ord($c) >= self::ORD_SPACE) {
4214:                     return $c;
4215:                 }
4216: 
4217:                 return ' ';
4218:             }
4219: 
4220:             /**
4221:              * Is $c a letter, digit, underscore, dollar sign, or non-ASCII character.
4222:              *
4223:              * @return bool
4224:              */
4225:             protected function isAlphaNum($c) {
4226:                 return ord($c) > 126 || $c === '\\' || preg_match('/^[\w\$]$/', $c) === 1;
4227:             }

4229:             /**

4234:              * @uses get()
4235:              * @uses peek()
4236:              * @return string
4237:              */
4238:             protected function min() {
4239:                 if (0 == strncmp($this->peek(), "\xef", 1)) {
4240:                         $this->get();
4241:                         $this->get();
4242:                         $this->get();
4243:                 }
4244:

4247:

4273:

4275:                                     if ($this->isAlphaNum($this->b)) {
4276:                                         $this->action(self::ACTION_KEEP_A);

4283:

4288:                                         $this->action(self::ACTION_KEEP_A);

4313:                                             }

4327:             /**
4328:              * Get the next character, skipping over comments. peek() is used to see
4329:              * if a '/' is followed by a '/' or '*'.
4330:              *
4331:              * @uses get()
4332:              * @uses peek()
4333:              * @throws JSMinException On unterminated comment.
4334:              * @return string
4335:              */
4336:             protected function next() {
4337:                 $c = $this->get();
4338: 
4339:                 if ($c === '/') {
4340:                     switch($this->peek()) {
4341:                         case '/':
4342:                             for (;;) {
4343:                                 $c = $this->get();
4344: 
4345:                                 if (ord($c) <= self::ORD_LF) {
4346:                                     return $c;
4347:                                 }
4348:                             }
4349: 
4350:                         case '*':
4351:                             $this->get();
4352: 
4353:                             for (;;) {
4354:                                 switch($this->get()) {
4355:                                     case '*':
4356:                                         if ($this->peek() === '/') {
4357:                                             $this->get();
4358:                                             return ' ';
4359:                                         }
4360:                                         break;
4361: 
4362:                                     case null:
4363:                                         throw new JSMinException('Unterminated comment.');
4364:                                 }
4365:                             }
4366: 
4367:                         default:
4368:                             return $c;
4369:                     }
4370:                 }
4371: 
4372:                 return $c;
4373:             }
4374: 
4375:             /**

4377:              *
4378:              * @uses get()
4379:              * @return string|null
4380:              */
4381:             protected function peek() {
4382:                 $this->lookAhead = $this->get();
4383:                 return $this->lookAhead;
4384:             }
